Current Commentary

American Cotton and National Cotton

This time, the US$50 million American cotton and wheat loan stipulates that four-fifths will be used to purchase cotton and one-fifth to purchase wheat. This cotton and wheat are agricultural products for which China is currently experiencing a price drop. Among them, cotton is the only raw material for China's national industry yarn factories. Therefore, the impact will naturally have a great relationship with the national livelihood issue.

In the past year, the price of American cotton has fallen to around four cents, setting a new low record in nearly a hundred years. At the beginning of this loan, the authorities originally intended to take advantage of this low price to absorb a large amount of raw materials to develop China's cotton industry. However, based on the facts of today, it is definitely not what the authorities expected. Since Roosevelt took office, he has refused monetary agreements externally and implemented currency inflation internally. In just a few months, general prices have risen by more than double. Even considering the recent price of American cotton, it has reached about one dime. And American farmers in the South are still demanding higher cotton prices. Therefore, the former cotton price of four or five cents is probably no longer available today. Secondly, the intention of China to borrow cotton and wheat may be due to the large amount of cotton and wheat imported in the previous year. It is assumed that there will be the same amount of imports in the future. Therefore, it is thought that it is better to borrow on credit than to buy with cash. The intention is not wrong. However, the actual situation is different. The large import of cotton and wheat in the previous year was a unique phenomenon after China's great flood. And although the number of American cotton imported each year is quite large, most of it is consumed by foreign-owned factories in China. Among them, Japanese factories consume the most. Looking at these facts, this US$50 million cotton and wheat loan is worthy of research on the interests of China itself.

The first batch of cotton will soon be shipped from the west coast of the Pacific. When this first batch of cotton is about to arrive in port, the authorities must have pre-determined methods of control and management for the sake of national interest and the people's livelihood. And we especially hope that this method of control and management can be practical, appropriate, and beneficial to the people's livelihood.

Today, anyone with a little insight knows that the day American cotton arrives in port is the time when the price of national cotton will plummet. This can also be said to be an inevitable phenomenon in the future based on the principle of supply and demand in economics. After the price of Chinese national cotton plummets, the cotton farmers who will be directly and adversely affected will be most of them. The misfortune of harming farmers due to cheap grain last year is an example. Secondly, after the national cotton price plummets, the Japanese will definitely rise up and absorb a large amount of Chinese cotton to compensate for the loss of resisting Indian cotton after the abrogation of the Japan-India trade treaty and to use it as a tool to manipulate the price of Chinese cotton in the future. On the yarn factory side in our country, after being affected by the plummeting of national cotton, the yarn price must become lower and lower, then the foundation of our yarn factories will also 形搖動 (be shaken). Based on the actual situation, it is difficult for Hua factories to consume this US$40 million of cotton. As a result, most of it will fall into the hands of foreign factories in China and strengthen their competitiveness against our yarn factories invisibly.

Therefore, before this American cotton arrives in port, appropriate control methods must be planned in advance. The government, yarn factories, and financial circles should work together as soon as possible to save the crisis of the yarn factories' future and avoid increasing the suffering of the people in the future. We borrow chopsticks to plan, the first step should be taken by the yarn factories and the government to maintain the price of Chinese national cotton, so as not to fall due to the arrival of American cotton. Only then can Chinese cotton farmers be slightly spared from innocent disasters and reduce the covetous hearts of foreign merchants. The second step should be taken by the government and the financial community to raise funds to stockpile American cotton, on the one hand, so that American cotton will not disrupt the market of Chinese national cotton, and on the other hand, to reduce the power of foreign factories to manipulate and oppress. In short, this issue is very important today. It is not too late to mend the fold after a sheep has been lost. We dare to contribute our own views. If the parties concerned can pay attention to it, it will not only be the fortune of cotton farmers and yarn factories.

The Hopei Peace Preservation Corps Prepares to Counterattack Funing

Su Yukun Ordered to Proceed to Yuguan

Negotiating with the Japanese Regarding Bandit Suppression Matters

Changli Under Strict Guard

Liu Xingpei Arrives in Tianjin to Report the Loss of the City

(Beiping) The notorious bandit leader of Luandong, "Old Mouse," led his forces to besiege Funing County. On the 24th, they bombarded the city, causing severe damage to civilian houses. Our Peace Preservation Corps resisted. Suddenly, a Japanese man named Kunihiro Ryokichi, claiming to be the captain of the "Manchukuo" border police, led cavalry to demand entry into the city to protect County Magistrate Liu Xingpei. The city gates were opened, and bandit troops gradually entered the city, occupied civilian residences, and engaged in rampant looting. Liu and Public Security Bureau Chief Wu Jinrong retreated to Changli Railway Station that night. Refugees fled in droves. Liu, Wu, and other county government officials arrived in Tianjin last night to report the fall of the county to Yu Xuezhong. Yu telegraphed He Yingqin and Yin Tong in Beiping yesterday afternoon, and stated that it had been determined that the "Manchukuo" police captain who demanded entry into the city was not Japanese. Yin Tong, acting on He's orders, telegraphed Su Yukun, the special commissioner stationed in Tianjin for negotiations, to meet with Yu this afternoon. Our side has decided to dispatch the Peace Preservation Corps to counterattack, and ordered Su Yukun to proceed to Yuguan immediately to negotiate with the Japanese regarding our bandit suppression efforts. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) A person from Yuguan reported that the "Old Mouse" bandit gang is entrenched in Liushouying, Qinhuangdao, Beidaihe, and other places, looting and harassing the population. They extorted a large sum of money from the Qinhuangdao Chamber of Commerce. The Chamber of Commerce raised and handed over 30,000 yuan, but the bandits continued their disturbances. Many civilians fled to Tianjin for refuge. Bandits were rampant near Yuguan. A small number even infiltrated the city and carried out looting, but were driven out by the local self-defense corps. Rumors were rampant in Yuguan, and people were restless. The "Old Mouse" bandit leader has led the majority of his forces across Yutian, heading towards Sanhe, attempting to move west to Shunyi and join forces with Fang Jun. The people of Changli, Funing, Sanhe, and other counties are living in misery. (26th Special Dispatch)

In Changli, there was heavy rain on the night of the 25th, and the situation eased slightly. It became slightly tense again after 8:00 AM on the 26th, but then returned to normal. It is reported that the vanguard of the bandit forces is stationed in the area near Liushouying. Our police force is guarding along the Changli border. However, a detachment of about 200 scattered bandits has already circled to the northwest of Changli, in the area east of Lulong, observing the bandit situation and still attempting to connect with Yutian. However, the source of the trouble is definitely in Qinhuangdao, so the situation is not optimistic, but there is no need to be pessimistic in the face of events, because the Second Peace Preservation Corps will arrive in Changli to reinforce us, so morale is very high, and we will take the opportunity to take Funing city in one fell swoop. Currently, since the city was lost, half of the civilians have not been able to escape, and the bandit forces are committing adultery, looting, and all kinds of atrocities everywhere, so cases of hanging and drowning are endless. The puppet County Magistrate Zu Guoqin has been actively recruiting local ruffians since Liu left the city. After County Magistrate Liu arrived in Changli, he was at headquarters for a time, but did not return on the night of the 25th for some reason. On the 26th, he received an order from the province to be transferred back to Tianjin. Changli has been quite panicked for days due to the loss of Funing City. Unscrupulous elements took the opportunity to spread rumors, so the situation in the streets is bleak, with few businesses open. In the afternoon, the county government convened a joint meeting of local gentry, and Corps Commander Dou made a special trip to participate, clearly stating his position on the spot and expressing his determination to absolutely maintain Changli, hoping that all sectors would live in peace and not disturb each other. Therefore, people's hearts have gradually settled down. Many people have visited Dou in recent days. An American pastor visited on the 25th, and Dou explained that he was determined to maintain order with all his strength, ensuring that there would be no danger. On the morning of the 26th, Kawai, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Luanzhou, also came to Changli to inspect the streets and four gates, and then asked Dou many questions. He reported to Qin Fang based on what he was told. In the afternoon, Li Jichun sent personnel to Changli to inquire about the bandit suppression situation. As of midnight, there were no major changes in any direction, but the dangerous situation remained. The refugees who came to Changli have been taken in by all sectors in the newly established Women and Children Relief Association. It is heard that more than thirty infants have drowned along the way. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Su Yuqi, the representative sent by Yin Tong to Changchun for negotiations, arrived in Tianjin from Beiping at 7:30 PM on the 15th. He first met with Nakamura, the Japanese commander stationed in Tianjin, and then went to Yuguan to meet with Ochi-gawa, the garrison commander, to ask them not to interfere in the bandit suppression. If successful, Yu Xuezhong will increase the number of Peace Preservation Corps by 2,000 to vigorously suppress bandits in Luandong. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Funing County Magistrate Liu Xingpei, along with Public Security Bureau Chief Wu Jinrong, Education Bureau Chief Zheng Buyuan, Finance Bureau Chief Zhao Xingren, Construction Bureau Chief Sun Xuewen, and the seals and important files, arrived in Tianjin on the morning of the 26th and set up a temporary office at the Qiyun Hotel. At 10:00 AM, Liu and the four bureau chiefs visited Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong to report on the loss of the city and asked to be punished. Liu told reporters that the bandits who attacked Funing numbered only one or two thousand. Japanese and Korean ruffians secretly provided military fire. If it were not for the restraint of harming valued objects, they would be easily defeated. He is quietly awaiting Chairman Yu's orders. If he can send police to suppress bandits, he is willing to volunteer. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Bandits were discovered outside Changli City on the evening of the 26th, and the situation is serious. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The traitor Hao Peng was protected by the Japanese some days ago and went to Changchun via Dalian to engage in activities. Qinhuangdao, Liushouying, Haiyangzhen, Yuguanzhen, Taitouying, and other places are filled with bandits, and the people are suffering. The situation in Changli is critical, and a special curfew was imposed on the 25th. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Sources in the transportation sector report that it is not that the Luandong Peace Preservation Corps and the defense corps are incapable of suppressing bandits, but that every time they encircle and suppress them, just when they are about to succeed, they are constrained by the fear of harming valued objects, so there is no way to do it. The bandits are therefore gathering more and more. This time, more than twenty heavy trucks loaded military fire from Shijiazhuang to Funing to supply the bandits. After County Magistrate Liu Xingpei received assistance from the Tangshan Peace Preservation Corps, he repelled the bandits besieging the east, south, and west sides of the city on the evening of the 22nd. The bandits on the north side were also about to be captured, but the bandits obtained powerful reinforcements and returned on the morning of the 24th, reoccupying Zijin Mountain and firing more than fifty cannons into the city. The firing was extremely accurate. County Magistrate Liu Xingpei retreated to Changli at 10:00 PM on the 24th, along with Peace Preservation Corps Commander Dou Xizhe, Public Security Bureau Chief Wu Jinrong, and others. The bandits then entered Funing, burning, looting, and raping, a truly unprecedented disaster. About 10,000 people risked their lives to escape to Changli, and more than 20,000 were unable to escape. On the 25th, local bullies and traitors organized an autonomous association and elected a puppet county magistrate. The bandit forces were divided into two routes and attacked Changli and Lulong. A thousand men from Shi Yousan's unit stationed in Yutian, a military headquarters, has dispatched Staff Officer Li to take roll call of them. It is heard that the unit is unstable and will respond to the "Old Mouse". According to an investigation by a certain party, Shi Yousan has not arrived in Tianjin, but only his partisans are unusually active in the Japanese concession, secretly organizing the East Asia Allied Army. (26th Special Dispatch)

Chaisaki Visits He to Express the Japanese Attitude

Denies Collusion with Fang Jixiang

The Japanese Army Prepares to Drive Out Fang's Troops

Preventing Fang Ji from Fleeing to Luandong

(Beiping) Chaisaki met with He Yingqin and stated that the Japanese army had not colluded with Fang Jixiang's army. The Japanese Kwantung Army will begin operations against Fang Jixiang's army entrenched in the Niulanshan area from the 27th, and will accommodate China's request to prevent them from fleeing to Luandong. The Kwantung Army will dispatch a large number of air squadrons to monitor the movements of Fang Jixiang's army in the Niulanshan and east of Huairou areas, and will use infantry to suppress and drive Fang Jixiang's army to attack in the southwest direction of the war zone, in order to seek a quick solution. The bandit army in Funing broke into the county seat, or posing as Japanese troops, to disturb the county seat. Chaisaki also guaranteed that no Japanese troops would enter the war zone. In the future, Chinese bandit suppression peace preservation teams may freely deal with bandit armies posing as Japanese troops. (26th Special Dispatch)

He hosted a banquet for Japanese General Sakata and Chaisaki, Nakayama, and others tonight, inviting Lei Shourong, Yin Tong, Li Zeyi, and others to accompany them. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) He Yingqin replied to reporters in writing that Military Attaché Chaisaki came to see him some days ago and relayed the Kwantung Army's opinion, saying that the Kwantung Army's reply telegram had arrived in Beiping and fully understood the disposition of Fang's troops. However, if Fang's troops still raised the anti-Japanese banner and did not withdraw from the demilitarized zone within the time limit, the Kwantung Army would still attack them. However, our side cannot accept this approach because Huairou is Chinese territory, and we still ask Chaisaki to relay to the Kwantung Army that our side will handle the matter. If Fang flees to Tianjin and Beiping, we will of course resolve it. The bandit suppression in Luandong has been handed over to the War Zone Receiving Committee and the Hopei Provincial Government to be responsible for. There are rumors that Fang's troops are advancing into Shunyi and Tang's troops are advancing into Changping, but this is not true. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yin Tong said that he met with Chaisaki this afternoon. He received a telegram from the Kwantung Army expressing its acceptance of preventing Fang Jixiang's army from fleeing east, and will begin operations tomorrow to seek a quick solution to Fang Jixiang's army.

The Japanese army and Fang Jixiang's army have repeatedly stated that there is no collusion. A unit of the Japanese army has arrived in Miyun and will be transported by car. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Chinese side of the North China regime claims that the current state of chaos is slanderous propaganda, saying that the recent disturbances in North China by the Japanese army instigating Fang Zhenwu, Ji Hongchang, and other bandits in North China is the first step in aggression. League of Nations Assembly and Disarmament Talks

Politicians from Various Countries Working on Two Fronts

Japan Dispatches Sato to Geneva

(Geneva) While the League of Nations Assembly is in session, politicians from various countries are discussing disarmament matters. British Foreign Secretary Simon visited Aloisi (Italy), Paul-Boncour (France), and Neurath (Germany) today. Disarmament issues were discussed during these meetings. French and German representatives have not yet engaged in direct talks. The Italian side seems willing to act as an intermediary. British circles hope that progress made in the next few days will allow concrete proposals to be submitted to the main body of the Disarmament Conference on October 15th. (Reuters, 25th)

(Geneva) Davis, the American representative to the Disarmament Conference, met with German Foreign Minister Neurath at dinner. Italian Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs Suvich and the country's representative to the League of Nations, Aloisi, also met with Neurath. The League of Nations Assembly held its second meeting in the afternoon and elected vice presidents. French Premier Daladier received 42 votes, with six votes mistakenly cast for French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour (as Paul-Boncour was not a candidate for re-election), which were also attributed to Daladier. German Foreign Minister Neurath received 40 votes, British Foreign Secretary Simon received 41 votes, and Persian Prince Foroughi received 39 votes. France's victory is considered settled. Committees were then organized. The German delegation requested that the issue of minority rights, listed on the agenda, be transferred to the Political Committee for consideration. This case will be discussed tomorrow. Germany has made it a habit to demand prompt public discussion of minority rights issues whenever the League of Nations convenes. The Chairman of the League of Nations Executive Council, Mowinckel, hosted a luncheon for his colleagues, but Paul-Boncour did not attend and was represented by Bérenger, the Chairman of the Foreign Affairs Committee of the French Senate. Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss met today with the Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans and the Dutch Foreign Minister de Graeff, and also arranged to meet with French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour tomorrow. (Havas, 25th)

(Geneva) Italian figures have already explored the German viewpoint on the principles proposed in the recent tripartite talks among Britain, France, and the United States in Paris. The intentions of Germany on this matter will soon be known to the governments of Britain, France, the United States, and Italy. (Havas, 25th)

(London) The non-permanent representatives of the League of Nations Executive Council from Guatemala, Ireland, and Norway are about to be re-elected. The Austrian government has probed the intentions of major European capitals, seemingly seeking to secure a seat. It is now heard that member states of the League of Nations have suggested to Britain that Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss be elected as one of the non-permanent representatives. Regarding the three vacancies for non-permanent representatives of the Executive Council, apart from Guatemala, which has been reserved for Latin American countries, Britain intends to propose Portugal and Australia as candidates for the other two seats. Although some have suggested to Britain that Portugal yield to Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss, Britain believes that if Dollfuss cannot remain in power for long, and Austrian politics fall into the hands of the National Socialist Party or a government based on National Socialism is established, this position of non-permanent representative will inevitably be transferred to a pro-German politician, resulting in a self-defeating outcome. Therefore, it does not support replacing Portugal with Austria. Thus, it is unlikely that the suggestion of Dollfuss as a candidate will be raised again in the near future. (Havas, 25th)

(Tokyo) Japan is not sending a representative to the current session of the League of Nations Council in Geneva, adhering to its policy of withdrawing from the League and maintaining political isolation. However, since the current League of Nations meeting appointed a committee for technical cooperation with China, and the Chinese delegation intends to use this opportunity to request a report on the handling of Sino-Japanese issues, Japan feels the need for caution. It has decided to dispatch Ito Jushi, the Vice-Director of the Japanese League of Nations Bureau, and Yokoyama Masayuki, a Counselor at the Embassy in Belgium, to Geneva. The Japanese government has recently decided to additionally dispatch Ambassador Sato, the Japanese Plenipotentiary to the Disarmament Conference, to Geneva to monitor the situation from the sidelines. Sato departed from Brussels, Belgium, on the 24th and is expected to arrive in Geneva on the 26th. (Nichi-Ren, 26th)

(Geneva) The warning issued by Norwegian Prime Minister Mowinckel about the pervasive possibility of war shocked the League of Nations Assembly, which opened today. Mowinckel, newly elected as Chairman of the League of Nations Executive Council, continued after issuing his warning, stating that the Four-Power Pact recently signed by Germany, Italy, France, and Britain could greatly contribute to the maintenance of order in Europe, but that freedom of thought and individual liberty were not sufficiently protected in various parts of Europe. (Reuters, 25th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly traditionally establishes six committees: (1) the Organization and Legal Matters Committee, (2) the Finance and Economics Committee, (3) the Disarmament Committee, (4) the Budget and Administration Committee, (5) the Humanitarian and Social Issues Committee, and (6) the Political Issues Committee. This year's Assembly, due to the ongoing Disarmament Conference, did not establish the third committee. Among the remaining five committees, two have already decided on their agendas today. The second committee, namely the Finance and Economics Committee, has elected the Belgian representative, Viénot, as Chairman and the Venezuelan representative, Parra, as Vice Chairman and has decided that the various issues related to the committee should be reviewed in the following order: (1) the work of industrial organization, (2) the work of transportation and transit organization, and (3) economic and financial work. In addition, the sixth committee, namely the Political Issues Committee, chaired by the Spanish representative, Madariaga, passed the following agenda: (1) the Nansen International Refugee Office, (2) the issue of slavery, (3) cooperation between newspapers and peace organizations, and (4) international intellectual cooperation. Apart from the meetings of the above committees, the representatives of the signatory countries of the Four-Power Pact engaged in extensive activities this morning, with Davis, the American representative to the Disarmament Conference, and Henderson, the Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, participating. Henderson plans to leave Geneva for a few days tomorrow and intends to facilitate informal meetings among the representatives of the countries most relevant to the disarmament issue before his departure, so that countries can reach a consensus on principles based on the draft disarmament treaty. However, it is reported that no concrete results have yet been achieved in this regard. (Havas, 26th)

Argentina Rejoins League of Nations

The Argentine Congress in Buenos Aires unanimously passed a resolution today to rejoin the League of Nations, with the reservation that the understanding of Article 21 of the League Covenant regarding the protection of territorial integrity, similar to the Monroe Doctrine, remains valid. Argentina's declaration of reservation stated that the Monroe Doctrine is merely a unilateral political declaration and cannot constitute an understanding of territorial integrity. Argentina withdrew from the League of Nations in 1920. (Reuters, 26th)

National Government Hires American Engineer to Assist in Road Construction Planning

Glenn from New York State

A newspaper here in Albany reports reliable sources stating that the Chinese government has invited Glenn, a member of the New York State Public Works Commission, to China to oversee road construction. It is said that the Chinese government has raised substantial funds and plans to build 22,000 miles of new-style roads, hiring renowned road construction engineer Glenn to assist in road construction planning and oversee the works. When asked about this news today, Glenn declined to comment, leading many to believe that Glenn has indeed received an invitation from the Chinese government. Glenn first served as a member of the New York State Road Commission in 1919 and is currently engaged in a $40 million road construction project in this state. According to sources within the New York State Governor's office, if China does invite Glenn, he will be granted leave to go to China. However, sources within the office declined to confirm the authenticity of this news. Other sources have also stated that building 22,000 miles of roads would require hiring engineers for several years. (National News Agency, 25th)

(Berlin) Zhang Xueliang has been quite busy with social engagements during his ten days here. He departed for Copenhagen, the capital of Denmark, this morning. While in Germany, Zhang met with Prussian Prime Minister Goering and attended several official banquets, inspected infantry, artillery, and aviation schools, and visited various industries, with a particular focus on the Krupp factory, where he spent the end of the week. Japan Establishes Military's Dictatorial Power

Expanding the Authority of the Chief of the Military General Staff

New Regulations to Be Implemented Next Month

(Tokyo) The new regulations revised by the Japanese Military General Staff will be announced tomorrow and implemented from October 1st. Its purpose is to cope with the precarious situation of 1936 and to establish the dictatorial power of the military. The main points of its contents are as follows: (1) The title of the Chief of the Military General Staff will be changed to Chief of the General Staff, with a Vice Chief assisting in his duties, appointed by the Emperor. (2) The Chief of the General Staff will be in charge of national defense, military deployment, and operational matters. (3) The Commander of the Combined Fleet, the commanders of various fleets, and the commander of the puppet state's navy will be directly under the Emperor. The various commanders will be supervised by the Navy Minister regarding military administration and will be directed by the Chief of the General Staff in terms of operations, but military actions within the area of operations will be determined by the commander. (4) The personnel of each department will be called staff officers. (5) Military attachés will be stationed in major embassies. (6) The service regulations for the department members will be determined by the Chief of the General Staff. (Hua-Lian, 26th)

Illegal Buying and Selling Negotiations Stalled

Japanese Puppets Deliberately Disrupting the Administration of the Chinese Eastern Railway

Key Russian Officials Continue to Be Arrested

Russian Consul-General in Harbin Lodges Another Protest

(Tokyo) Illegal negotiations regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway have completely stalled due to the puppet regime's large-scale arrest of Russian railway staff and key administrative personnel. According to Japanese sources, the puppet state's direct actions against Russia will gradually expand. The ultimate outcome is difficult to predict at this time. (Hua-Lian, 26th)

(Harbin) The director of the Machinery Department of the Chinese Eastern Railway Administration, Garina, the station masters of Manchouli and Boli stations, and five others, who were summoned by the "Manchukuo" police authorities due to the exposure of illegal incidents, are temporarily detained pending the completion of the interrogation. Due to the summoning of the station masters, the staff at Boli Station were shaken. The international train departing from the station on the morning of the 24th was delayed for several hours because there was no departure order from the station master. (Dentsu, 26th)

(Harbin) Several more people related to the Chinese Eastern Railway have now been arrested. Rumors circulating about the arrest of Chinese Eastern Railway employees Garina, Raflov, Kubeli, and Abalov on the 24th of this month, claiming that their arrest was the first step in the "Manchu" side's occupation of the Chinese Eastern Railway, have been officially denied by the authorities here. The "Manchu" authorities stated that their detention was related to the matter of withdrawing 79 locomotives into Russia, so they were temporarily detained. Yesterday, the Suifenhe station master, the freight depot director, the Manchouli station master, the owner of the Nikitinsky Hotel, and several others were arrested and will be sent to Harbin. In addition, an accountant, whose name has not been announced, was also detained for illegal expenditures. The Russian Consul-General here, Slavutsky, lodged a protest today. Shiruben replied that the arrest of the Russian personnel of the Chinese Eastern Railway was not because they were Soviet Russian citizens, but because they were criminal employees, hence the arrest. At present, railway operations have been suspended. (Reuters, 26th)

(Tokyo) The Soviet Russian Ambassador to Japan has protested to the Japanese government regarding the arrest of several Chinese Eastern Railway employees. Foreign Minister Hirota agreed to forward the protest to the "Manchu" government but said nothing else. A Foreign Ministry spokesman stated definitively today that the "Manchukuo" judiciary is completely independent, unlike China or Soviet Russia. (Reuters, 26th)

(Moscow) The Soviet Russian political circles are greatly troubled by the statement of the Japanese Foreign Ministry spokesman that the Japanese government is unaware of the arrears of military transport fees owed to the Chinese Eastern Railway. German Reporters Ordered to Leave the Country Within Three Days

And All Russian Newspaper Representatives in Germany Recalled

(Berlin) Recently, Mrs. Katz, a reporter for the Soviet government newspaper Izvestia, and Mr. Pesparov, a reporter for TASS, were arrested by the Chief of Police of Leipzig while reporting on the fire incident at the German Parliament Building. They were released after the intervention of the secretary of the Soviet Embassy. The governments of Russia and Germany have now had a disagreement over this matter. The Soviet government has recalled all Russian newspaper representatives stationed in Germany and ordered German journalists within its borders to leave Russian territory within three days, no later than the 29th of this month. This decision was communicated to the German authorities today. According to the Soviet side, the attitude adopted by the German National Socialist government towards the representatives of Soviet Russian newspapers, especially the arrest of Mrs. Katz and Mr. Pesparov, and the prohibition of other Soviet journalists from entering the court to listen to the proceedings, are the reasons for the Soviet government's decision. The Soviet Embassy in Germany lodged an oral protest with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on Saturday and Sunday of last week and indicated that the Soviet government intended to take retaliatory measures if necessary, but as of now, the German government believes that a response is unnecessary. (Havas, 26th)

The current situation seems difficult. The administration's overall air defense plan has been drafted, and the training of the core air defense team has begun. After three months, they will be able to graduate. After that, the core team will be distributed to various cities to be responsible for guiding the public. Guangdong Rice Merchants Temporarily Suspend Rice Imports

(Hong Kong) Guangdong rice merchants have temporarily suspended rice imports since the 24th. Rice merchants in Chencun and Jiangmen have also telegraphed the province to stop operations. Qu Fangpu was originally scheduled to attend the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the 26th to explain the foreign rice tax, but temporarily changed to send section chief Fang Dehua to attend. (Guangzhou) According to news from the Pioneer News Agency, District Finance Director Qu Fangpu declared at this morning's memorial week event that the collection of the new foreign rice tax aims to protect farmers from competition and enable farmers to improve their lives. Farmers in Guangdong Province have suffered greatly in recent years due to foreign rice competition. Although rice prices have been lowered, imports cannot be stopped. China spends huge sums of money each year to purchase foreign grain, and if this continues, the nation's wealth will be exhausted. The revenue from the foreign rice tax will be used entirely to improve agricultural affairs and the living conditions of farmers. The Chairman of Guangxi Province has telegraphed the Guangdong authorities, expressing support for the collection of the foreign rice tax and stating that Guangxi Province plans to transport grain to aid Guangdong Province to avoid food shortages for the people, and finally urged rice merchants to awaken quickly and not oppose the tax. The Guangdong Engineering Union has also expressed support for the authorities to implement this tax in order to stop foreign goods competition. The Finance Department will meet with representatives of the Guangdong Chamber of Commerce tomorrow to explain the reasons for collecting this new tax. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

Why was the allocation method changed, with the emergency relief and work-relief funds reduced to 1.5 million yuan each, while 1 million yuan was allocated for medical and miscellaneous expenses? (2) How can 1.5 million yuan for work-relief manage the Yellow River? (3) The central government stipulates that expenses for relief funds shall not exceed 0.2% of the relief funds. Therefore, the expenses for 4 million yuan of relief funds should not exceed 8,000 yuan. Is it not excessive that the medical expenses amount to 992,000 yuan? (4) American cotton and wheat should account for 30% of the funds used for construction and rural relief. However, no construction is more important than managing the Yellow River. Throughout history, only managing the Yellow River has been mentioned, not managing the Yangtze River. Over 60 million yuan has been spent on managing the Yangtze River in 20 years. Now, 10 million yuan is allocated for managing the Yellow River, but there is no guarantee. Several dozens of counties in the three provinces have been flooded. Rural relief should prioritize the three provinces. (26th Dispatch)

Dalian Corpse Box Case

Japanese Manhunt for a Love Murderer

(Dalian) Yesterday, the police discovered a box containing a dismembered corpse. The box had been hidden in Ms. Yokoyama's residence for twenty days. The police quickly identified the deceased as Soyagi and the murderer as Nakayoo. Ms. Yokoyama is the murderer's lover. Ms. Yokoyama has now been arrested and confessed that the deceased and the murderer were rivals in love and were murdered on September 5 at the home of Mr. and Mrs. Kodama. Dr. Kodama is the head of the pathology department of the South Manchuria Railway and enjoys a good reputation. Ms. Yokoyama also stated that the murderer, after killing his rival, placed the body in a box and sent it to her house for hiding. Whether the two met at the Kodama's house by chance or by premeditation cannot be determined. The two were competing for Dr. Kodama's wife. The wife initially had an affair with the murderer, then abandoned him and fell in love with the deceased, which led to this love murder case. Mr. and Mrs. Kodama witnessed the event at the time. After the incident, the wife left for Japan. The police have telegraphed Japan to request her arrest. The murderer has not yet been apprehended, and the police believe that he has left Dalian or is hiding in Shanghai. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

Hurricane and Earthquake

Hurricane Strikes Gulf of Mexico Again

Tampico City Reduced to Rubble

Earthquake on the Adriatic Coast

Italy and Serbia Simultaneously Suffer Disasters

Mexico City The famous Mexican oil port of Tampico has been directly hit by hurricanes twice within ten days. Three-quarters of the port has been reduced to rubble. According to statistics from the Ministry of Interior, the death toll is close to 300, with more than 2,000 injured. Streets are still flooded, and losses are estimated to be in the millions. Upon receiving the report, the government immediately dispatched army planes to investigate. It is reported that the entire port is half-submerged, and traffic is cut off. A plane rescue team is being organized to transport food and medicine for relief. The hurricane suddenly broke out in the Gulf of Mexico, with the rain changing direction and hitting Tampico directly with winds of 100 miles per hour. There was no preparation beforehand, so a torrential rain poured down, and the tide rose on the shore. Houses that were not firmly built collapsed or were washed away by the flood, resulting in many deaths and injuries. More small boats were lost. As the hurricane blew inland, mountain torrents poured down, many fields and houses were washed away, railroads were interrupted, and oil fields were submerged. The scale of the disaster is unprecedented in the history of the port. The local authorities have announced martial law to prevent looting after the flood recedes. (25th Kuomintang News)

(New York) According to the latest news about the Tampico storm, the death toll is as high as 5,000, and the horrifying news of the disaster is gradually spreading. It is reported that three-quarters of the entire territory of Tampico has been wiped out, with losses reaching millions of dollars. (25th Reuters Dispatch)

Mexico City According to the latest news from Tampico, all buildings in the city have been almost completely destroyed by the hurricane, and it is feared that hundreds of people have been buried in the rubble. (26th Havas Dispatch)

Rome Italy today experienced the most severe earthquake in years, with at least eight deaths and more than 150 injuries. The worst affected area was the Abruzzo Mountains in central Italy. Two consecutive earthquakes occurred at 4:36 this morning, lasting half a minute, causing many houses to collapse. Rescue teams are currently digging in the ruins to retrieve buried people. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

Rome A violent earthquake occurred this morning along the Adriatic coast. The intensity was greatest in the Abruzzo and Molise provinces of Italy, and the situation within Yugoslavia was likely no less severe than in these two provinces. The government has dispatched trains and airplanes to transport relief supplies to the disaster areas. The major earthquake began at 4:30, but at 5:30, the Naples Observatory still reported earthquakes. The most intense quake lasted ten seconds, followed by successive tremors, and the momentum seemed to subside slightly. However, it caused significant damage in Yugoslavia. The Adriatic coast suffered the most. Naples, Scara, Teramo, Agulha, and Masilla were the first to report disasters. Fortunately, there were no casualties. Subsequently, Trieste reported that after the earthquake in the lowlands near Rubellara in Yugoslavia, heavy rains followed, and the disaster was extremely severe. Many houses collapsed, and many villagers died. In Italy, the county of Chieti was the most severely affected, with many deaths. (26th Kuomintang News)

Rome A severe earthquake occurred in Abruzzo, Italy, at 4:35 this morning. The affected area is still not determined, but its center is approximately on the line connecting Sulmona and Pescara. Rome also experienced a significant earthquake. The death toll and injuries are likely to be high, and the material losses will certainly be huge. From Monday night to Tuesday, earthquakes were also felt near Muelheim and Badenweiler in southern Germany. (26th Kuomintang News)

Puppet Organization Sacrifices Northeast Railway Rights

- Puppet Ministry of Transportation Signs Secret Agreement with Japan -

South Manchuria Railway Company Seizes Operating Rights on All Lines

Totaling Seventeen Lines, 3,495 Kilometers in Length

It has been over two years since the Northeast fell. Not only have the lands of the four provinces been occupied by the violent Japanese, but also the state-owned railways in the Northeast have been sold by the puppet organization to the Japanese South Manchuria Railway Company. We have obtained various documents related to the puppet organization's sale of state-owned railways in the Northeast, statistics on the railways seized, the secret agreement signed by Japan and the puppet organization, and the recent status of the puppet organization's construction of over 40,000 li of highways in the Northeast, which are compiled below to inform our compatriots who are concerned about the Northeast's railway administration.

Full Text of the Puppet Organization's Sale of Railway Rights

On March 1 of this year (i.e., the second year of the puppet Datong), which is also the anniversary of the complete occupation of our Northeast state-owned railways, Ding Jianshou, the puppet Minister of Transportation, issued an order to announce the transfer of the Northeast railways (listed below) to the South Manchuria Railway Company, owned by Japan, for management and operation. The instructions and announcements are as follows: (1) Instruction No. 44: "To comply with the order, it is hereby ordered that the railways (railway names listed below) and their affiliated businesses in Announcement No. 7 of the Ministry of Transportation, have been entrusted to the South Manchuria Railway Company for operation since February 9 of the second year of Datong (i.e., 1933). You must comply with this order." (2) Announcement No. 7: "For the purpose of announcement, this Ministry has entrusted the state-owned railways and various affiliated businesses to the South Manchuria Railway Company for operation since February 9 of the second year of Datong. This is hereby announced." (3) The puppet Ministry of Transportation issued a document to various railway bureaus stating, "In compliance with the puppet order, the government and the South Manchuria Railway Company have signed an agreement for the entrusted operation of state-owned railways and associated businesses (including the Songhua River waterway business). All staff members of the relevant bureaus must be subordinate to the Railway General Bureau and continue to serve in their positions from February 9 of the second year of Datong. All rights and obligations previously held by the staff members for their respective railways shall be inherited and handled by the Railway General Bureau. You are hereby informed and instructed to inform."

Full Text of the Japan-Puppet Organization Agreement

Article 1: The government of Manchukuo owes the South Manchuria Railway Company a total of approximately 130 million gold yuan in loans. To guarantee this total amount, the already completed railways of Jichang, Jidun, Jihai, Siping-Taonan, Taonan-Angangxi, Taonan-Suosuo, Qiqihar-Koshi, Hulan-Hailun (including a part of the Songhua River waterway business), Shenyang-Hailong, Fengshan (including the Datong Line and affiliated ports), and all assets and income associated with these railways are entrusted to the South Manchuria Railway Company for operation. Article 2: In the event of existing debt relationships between the government of Manchukuo and third parties other than the South Manchuria Railway Company, the South Manchuria Railway Company shall handle them after consultation between the government and the South Manchuria Railway Company. The necessary payments and the repayment funds for the loans of the "Fengshan Line" to the British-Chinese Company shall be paid from the income earned by the South Manchuria Railway Company after the entrusted operation. Also, the "Fengshan" Railway, related to the British-Chinese Company loan, shall not be used as a guarantee for this loan until the loan is resolved. Article 3: The government of Manchukuo shall separately contract the South Manchuria Railway Company to construct the Dunhua-Tumen River Railway, the Lafa-Harbin Railway, and the Taidong-Harbin Railway. The construction cost of these three routes is approximately 100 million gold yuan in total. Furthermore, regarding the aforementioned construction of the Dunhua-Tumen River Railway, Manchukuo should acquire the Tumen River Railway, and Manchukuo shall borrow approximately 6 million gold yuan from the South Manchuria Railway Company as acquisition funds, and also entrust the South Manchuria Railway Company with the operation of this light railway. Article 4: On the same day as the signing of the agreement, the Manchukuo side must publish the Railway Law. The main purpose of this Railway Law is to establish the principle of state-owned railways. The Railway Appropriation Law adopts the principle that all railways belong to the state. According to this law, the Shenyang-Hailong, Hulan-Hailun, and Qiqihar-Koshi lines are nationalized to unify the situation for the South Manchuria Railway Company to operate them. The above four articles shall be observed by both the Japanese and Manchu governments. The effective period is set at twenty years.

After the puppet Ministry of Transportation sold the railways to the South Manchuria Railway Company and signed an agreement with Japan, fearing public opposition, it specifically announced the reasons for the so-called entrusted operation as follows: First, Manchukuo, in order to ensure its security and develop its transportation business, especially regarding the national railway business, is an urgent task that cannot be delayed. Second, the current small railways in Manchukuo are independent and their operations are different, which is not conducive to substantial benefits and is not a unified transportation method. Moreover, before the national railway network plan is fully implemented, the current railways should be unified to seek reasonable operation and achieve economic, technical, and efficient goals. Third, Manchukuo's entrustment of the national railways to the South Manchuria Railway Company for unified operation is based on technical considerations, as the South Manchuria Railway Company has many years of experience and is most suitable. Fourth, the government of Manchukuo owes the South Manchuria Railway Company a huge debt of 130 million yuan. Based on the convenience of both parties, it is appropriate for the creditor to entrust the operation.

The Railway Law Announced by the Puppet Organization

The puppet organization's Railway Law was announced by the puppet Minister of Transportation Ding Jianshou in early July of this year with a ministerial order as follows: (1) Railways are state-owned, but railways for general transportation purposes, mainly for local transportation, and railways that are not for general transportation may not be state-owned. (2) To achieve the purpose of state ownership, all necessary railways may be appropriated. The railways to be appropriated, the date of appropriation, compensation, and other matters shall be determined separately. (3) The provisions of the preceding article shall apply to the appropriation of businesses associated with railways. (4) The gauge of state-owned railways shall be 1 meter, 4 decimeters, 3 centimeters, and 5 millimeters wide. However, railways that are not for general transportation may not comply with this dimension. (5) Regarding Article 1, the provisions that railways that are not state-owned shall be determined separately. (6) This law shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Methods of Utilizing Railways by the Puppet Organization

The following are the methods by which Ding Jianxiu, the puppet Minister of Transportation, simultaneously took over the Shenhai, Huhai, and Qike railways: (1) The government, in accordance with Articles 2 and 3 of the Railway Law, shall take over the railways belonging to the Shenhai Railway Company, the Huhai Railway Company, and the Qike Railway Engineering Bureau, and all related businesses; (2) The date of taking over the railways and related businesses in the preceding article shall be designated by the government; (3) The determination of the compensation price shall be negotiated with each company, and the organization of the review committee shall be determined separately; (4) On the date of the takeover, the government shall inherit the rights and obligations of the company's existing railways and related businesses, but the rights and obligations of borrowed funds shall not be limited; if the borrowed funds in the preceding paragraph are secured by the railway or its related businesses, the government shall inherit the rights and obligations of the borrowed funds; (5) The compensation for the takeover shall be delivered in the form of 6% national bonds to be repaid within 50 years, based on the price determined in Article 3, with any fraction less than 50 yuan calculated as 50 yuan; (6) From the date of the takeover to the date of delivery of the national bonds, the government shall pay the company an equivalent amount at the rate of 6% per annum on the takeover compensation; (7) The government may issue public bonds to the extent necessary for the execution of the takeover; (8) This law shall come into effect from the date of its promulgation.

The National Government Promulgates Civil Servant Ranks and Salaries

Effective from November 1st

Previous tables and regulations repealed on the same day

The Provisional Table of Civil Servant Ranks and Salaries has been promulgated by the National Government and is stipulated to be effective from November 1st of this year. The salary tables and regulations promulgated in the 16th and 18th years are repealed on the same day. The provisions and explanations of the provisional table are as follows:

(Rank Provisions) (1) National Government: Chief Civil Officer and Chief Accounting Officer, specially appointed; Bureau Chiefs, Secretaries, Accounting Officers, Councilors, Chief Statisticians, and Chief Accountants, senior appointment; Secretaries, Section Chiefs, Technicians, Statistics Directors, Accounting Directors, Section Staff, recommended appointment; Accountants, Statisticians, Technicians, First-Class Section Staff, First-Class Clerks, First-Class Staff Members, commissioned appointment. (2) Five Yuan and various ministries: Ministers and Chairmen, specially appointed; Vice Ministers, Vice Chairmen, Secretaries-General, Directors-General, Technical Supervisors, Auditors, Division Chiefs, Department Chiefs, Secretaries, Councilors, Technical Directors, Supervisors, Editors, Senior Editors, senior appointment; Secretaries, Section Chiefs, Coordinators, Technical Directors, Editors, Supervisors, Inspectors, Technicians, Section Chiefs, recommended appointment; First-Class Section Staff, Technicians, First-Class Technical Assistants, First-Class Clerks, First-Class Staff Members, commissioned appointment. (3) Provincial Governments and various departments: Provincial Chairmen, Department Chiefs, Commissioners, Secretaries-General, senior appointment; Secretaries, Section Chiefs, recommended appointment; First-Class Section Staff, First-Class Staff Members, commissioned appointment. (4) Municipal governments under the Executive Yuan and provincial governments: Mayors, Secretaries-General, Bureau Chiefs, Councilors, senior appointment; Mayors, Secretaries-General, Bureau Chiefs, Councilors, Secretaries, Section Chiefs, recommended appointment; Section Chiefs, Bureau Chiefs, Secretaries, First-Class Section Staff, First-Class Staff Members, commissioned appointment. (5) County governments and various bureaus: First-Class County Magistrates, senior appointment; First-Class County Magistrates, Second-Class County Magistrates, Third-Class County Magistrates, recommended appointment; Secretaries, Section Chiefs, Bureau Chiefs, County Supervisors, Section Staff, Staff Members, appointment.

(Salary Provisions) The salaries of officials at all levels in the National Government, the Five Yuan and various ministries, provincial governments and various departments, municipal governments under the Executive Yuan and various provinces, county governments and various bureaus are as follows: (1) Specially Appointed: 800 yuan; (2) Senior Appointment: First Grade 680 yuan, Second Grade 640 yuan, Third Grade 600 yuan, Fourth Grade 560 yuan, Fifth Grade 520 yuan, Sixth Grade 490 yuan, Seventh Grade 460 yuan, Eighth Grade 430 yuan; (3) Recommended Appointment: First Grade 400 yuan, Second Grade 380 yuan, Third Grade 360 yuan, Fourth Grade 340 yuan, Fifth Grade 320 yuan, Sixth Grade 300 yuan, Seventh Grade 280 yuan, Eighth Grade 260 yuan, Ninth Grade 240 yuan, Tenth Grade 220 yuan, Eleventh Grade 200 yuan, Twelfth Grade 180 yuan; (4) Commissioned Appointment: First Grade 200 yuan, Second Grade 180 yuan, Third Grade 160 yuan, Fourth Grade 140 yuan, Fifth Grade 130 yuan, Sixth Grade 120 yuan, Seventh Grade 110 yuan, Eighth Grade 100 yuan, Ninth Grade 90 yuan, Tenth Grade 85 yuan, Eleventh Grade 80 yuan, Twelfth Grade 75 yuan, Thirteenth Grade 70 yuan, Fourteenth Grade 65 yuan, Fifteenth Grade 60 yuan, Sixteenth Grade 55 yuan.

(Explanations) (1) If there are civil servants in various agencies who are not listed in this table but conform to the legal organization, the responsible officials of the agency shall refer to the equivalent personnel in this table, draft the appropriate grade and salary in detail, and report to the Ministry of Personnel for approval; (2) In areas with financial difficulties and lower living standards, the provincial and municipal governments may, based on the financial situation of the area, appropriately draft salary amounts according to the grades stipulated in this table, or reduce the payment, and report to the Ministry of Personnel for approval and record; (3) Those commissioned officials divided into three grades may be assigned the lowest grade salary for initial appointees; (4) Non-initial appointees may be assigned salaries according to their original grade in accordance with the second half of Article 12, paragraph 1 of the Appointment Law, but shall not exceed the highest grade salary of the corresponding official rank in this table; (5) Initial appointees shall be assigned the lowest grade salary of the corresponding official rank in this table in accordance with the first half of Article 12, paragraph 1 of the Appointment Law, but those who are promoted to official positions may be assigned grades based on the level of their original salary; (6) The grades and salaries of commissioners of various Yuan and committees shall be drafted by the respective agencies and reported to the Ministry of Personnel for approval; (7) If various agencies have secretaries commissioned at the recommended and appointed levels established in accordance with the organizational law, and their status is different from that of the various ministries, they shall be assigned salaries by referring to section chiefs and section staff and reported to the Ministry of Personnel for approval; (8) For inspectors, technical directors, technicians, and technical assistants in the various departments under the provincial government, the provincial government shall assign salaries by referring to section chiefs and section staff and report to the Ministry of Personnel for approval; (9) The grade and salary of mayors of various cities shall be drafted by the Executive Yuan or the provincial government within the scope stipulated in this table based on the circumstances of the respective municipal government and reported to the Ministry of Personnel for record; (10) The lowest grade salary of county magistrates and their assistants in various counties shall be drafted by the provincial governments within the scope stipulated in this table based on the circumstances of the respective counties and reported to the Ministry of Personnel for record; (11) The staff members stipulated in this table include special agents, clerks, telegraphers, file keepers, document clerks, and draftsmen, etc.; (12) The salary amounts in this table are in yuan.

(Yangzhou) Prison Warden Dismissed for Embezzling Prisoner Rations

Xi Binquan, the prison warden of Yizheng County under the jurisdiction of the Ninth Administrative District of Jiangsu, was found by the county government to have embezzled prisoner rations and reported to the High Court for handling. The High Court has now ordered Yizheng County to dismiss Xi from his position, hand him over to the political police for supervision, and appoint Wu Yongming to take over his duties. It also instructed the Ninth Administrative Commissioner's Office to investigate.

(Nantong) Thriving Flower Market in the Nantong and Taizhou Areas

In the Nantong and Taizhou areas of Jiangbei, the new cotton has recently been put on the market. This year's cotton production is abundant, and cotton merchants from various places in Jiangnan have come north to set up shops, and the market is very prosperous. Recently, cotton merchants negotiated with the Shanghai banking community and reached an agreement with China National Aviation Corporation to have planes flying the Shanghai-Ping route land at Nantong and Dongtai to deliver funds for purchasing cotton.

Provincial Bandit Criminals Resolved Separately

More than 50 criminals were escorted from Nantong to the provincial military court for trial. At this moment, three of the principal criminals, Lu Shifang and others, have been interrogated and executed, and the rest have also been resolved separately and sent to prison for execution. More than ten criminals whose cases have not been closed have been escorted back to the county provisional court for interrogation.

Changshu

The County Government Will Establish a Public People's Hospital

The county government recently saw that the fees charged by the local hospitals were too high, which was not a blessing for the common people. Therefore, there was an establishment of a public people's hospital. County Magistrate Zhou Heng and Yu Jiusi of the Red Cross Society have been working hard to plan and implement it. The funds are planned to be jointly borne by the county government and the Red Cross Society. It has been decided to hire one director, two assistant doctors, and a number of nurses. The address has been selected at the old site of the Ruying School on Baoben Street. In the future, it will start with helping ordinary people quit smoking. Outpatient visits for internal and external illnesses will be free of charge.

Jiangyin

Central Government Sends Personnel to Inspect Prisons

The Central Party Department has specially dispatched Cui Zixin and Yu Qi to investigate political prisoners in prisons in various counties. Commissioner Cui arrived in Cheng at 24:00 PM and immediately went to the county party headquarters, where they were received by Commissioner Xue Chan. They went to the county government to meet County Magistrate Ruan and accompanied them to the prison for investigation. They had individual conversations with the detained political prisoners, which lasted about two hours before it ended. At about 5:00 PM, they went to Wuxi.

Jiaxing

Burning Rice Stem Borer Eggs and Dead Seedlings

This year's rice stem borer in Jiaxing has spread quite severely, and many rice seedlings have dead hearts. The Rice Stem Borer Control Office has specially prepared and distributed bonuses to the villagers to encourage them to remove the dead-hearted seedlings and collect the rice stem borer eggs. As of now, more than 16,180,000 egg masses and dead-hearted seedlings have been sent from Xinfeng, Qihuang, Xinzha, Fengshi, Wangdian, Zhongdai, Hantang, Tanghui, Chengzhou and other districts, and more than 5,200 yuan in bonuses have been issued. The collected egg masses and seedlings were burned at the Children's Amusement Park on the 25th. Xu Guodong, the promotion director of the Provincial Entomology Bureau, and Zhu Jieshan, the instructor, came to He to supervise. Representatives from various agencies also attended the event.

Ningbo

Arresting Armed Bandits on the Chaoyang Ship

The Ningbo Detective Team received a secret report from an informant stating that an armed bandit named Zhang was hiding in the port, plotting illegal activities. After receiving the report, the team ordered detectives to investigate secretly. Sure enough, at 8:00 AM on the 23rd, on the Chaoyang ship off the Jiangbei Bund, the informant pointed out Zhang, and he was arrested. A six-inch Browning pistol with live ammunition was found next to him. After the team arrested Zhang, they also captured a suspect named Wang, who was serving as a militiaman, at the headquarters of the Fifth District Defense Corps of Yin County in Yangshan Hall on the Jiangbei Bund. In Dingxin Street in the city, they captured Chen Yangshi, the mistress of the bandit Zhang. Zhang confessed in the team that he had repeatedly committed kidnapping cases and also confessed that there were still four hostages hidden somewhere. Captain Yu Kangshu, considering the seriousness of the case, again requested the joint trial of the criminal by Administrative Commissioner Zhao Ci Sheng, Yin County Magistrate Chen Doulin, and Ningbo Public Security Bureau Chief Yu Jimin yesterday (the 24th). He then confessed the exact location where the hostages were hidden. After obtaining the confession, Commissioner Zhao personally led a squadron of the Police Brigade of the Public Security Bureau to the countryside to rescue the hostages and arrest the remaining bandits.

The Three Directors of the Disaster Relief Group of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association Departed Yesterday

Yang Zigong, Tang Mufen, and Cheng Jingsheng

According to Guowen News Agency, the National Government's Yellow River Flood Relief Committee has decided to form disaster relief, work relief, and health groups to carry out disaster relief. Xi Dejiong, the director of the disaster relief group, has decided to establish one investigation and release office each in Kaifeng, Henan, Daming, Hebei, and Jinan, Shandong, to first investigate the disaster situation and then handle the relief. Yesterday, the three directors of the investigation and release offices departed from Shanghai with their staff. Yang Zigong of Henan, Tang Mufen of Hebei, and Cheng Jingsheng of Shandong were originally work relief personnel from Shandong Province and have a lot of experience in river management. Yesterday, the reporter went to visit Mr. Xi Tongqing, an office worker of the association. According to him, the directors of the investigation and release offices have already departed. As for establishing branch offices in each disaster-stricken county, this will be done after the investigation and release offices are established and the situation is clarified. One branch office may be set up in one county, or two counties may jointly set up one branch office. No decision has been made yet. The budget for the disaster relief group is fixed at 1.5 million yuan, but matters such as purchasing relief supplies, setting up porridge kitchens, and accommodating refugees cannot be used to allocate funds, but rather funds must be raised based on the matter. Although the association has slightly fixed the allocation, it is only an approximate number. The continuous rain in Shanghai has nothing to do with the Yellow River, and recent telegrams have confirmed that the water level of the Yellow River is gradually receding. In short, disaster relief cannot be delayed, but the most important thing is for work relief to first block the breaches so that the people can live in peace and work can replace relief. However, at this time, the disaster relief, work relief, and health groups are all actively proceeding.

Zhou Xiangxian, the director of the work relief group of the association, believes that the breaches are waiting to be repaired and the victims are waiting for relief, and it is urgent to start work to block the breaches so that the people can live in peace and work can replace relief. He left Shanghai the night before last with Secretary Luo Dongli to go to Nanjing and, together with Song Xishang, the director of the engineering group, went to Shandong and Henan yesterday to conduct on-the-spot investigations and measurements. The internal organization of the work relief group consists only of administrative and engineering groups. Zhou himself serves as the director of the administrative group, and Song Xishang, the chief engineer of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, concurrently serves as the director of the engineering group. Since Zhou Xiangxian is the chairman of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, most of the personnel of the Yellow River Flood Relief Association's work relief group are transferred from the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission on a concurrent basis, so as to save expenses and rescue more victims.
