Essays

Cleverness

— Si Su

Modern people, after all, are not as good as ancient people, daring not to stray too far from the facts when speaking, are extremely clever: moreover, they understand each other tacitly, agreeing without prior consultation, only in being a clever method, everyone is self-taught, able to do it instinctively, it cannot be said that they are imitating, it is really because modern people all possess clever minds. Just like undeclared war, the Japanese are the most skilled at winning battles, as they did against Imperial Russia, ｜The date of the Russo-Japanese War was December 24, 1904, but in fact, on the 22nd, Japan had already begun military action, unexpectedly attacking Lushun and blockading it, thwarting the spirit of the Russian army. At the same time, the Combined Fleet attacked the Russian fleet anchored in Incheon, Korea, and also achieved a great victory, with the Russian ships completely destroyed. Japan first won victories on both sides, and then officially declared war on the 24th. The Russian Navy was defeated in Incheon Bay, and could hardly engage in naval warfare. It had to send a fleet from 8,000 miles away to fight, but it was defeated by the Japanese Navy, which waited leisurely, ambushing it in the Sea of Japan, resulting in a great defeat, and the outcome was decided. I remember that Russia once appealed to the international community for injustice, but the victor ultimately wins, who would blame Japan for not being honorable after its victory!! So too with us, ｜This does not only refer to the undeclared war of September 18th and January 28th. In the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, Japan also fought first and then declared war, the same as against Russia. ｜Thus, it won every battle. But this clever method is not only the forte of the Japanese, Bolivia and Paraguay are equally good at it. This is one. Another example is the propaganda of war reports, which is not only the forte of a certain country. Both Bolivia and Paraguay have deeply understood the essence of it, so the Bolivian-Paraguayan War, since it began more than a year ago, no one knows who is winning or losing. Recently, the National News Agency has another telegram, saying that according to Bolivian sources: the Bolivian army, under the command of German General Bidet, has repelled the attacking Paraguayan army; and on the same day, the Paraguayan government's war report also claimed: to have annihilated four regiments of Bolivian elite troops. The National News Agency can only transcribe the war reports of both sides, and cannot express an opinion on who is winning or losing. Journalists are still unclear about the actual war situation, and ordinary people are even more at a loss. Losing a battle is originally considered the most embarrassing thing by those involved. With this method, the shame of losing a battle is forever concealed, and instead, it is transformed into the most glorious "repelling" of the enemy, or "annihilating" the enemy. This is why it is called cleverness, I am afraid that even ancient people could not have dreamed of it!

Stone Fight

— Lanxi

When autumn arrives, I think again of the bad habits of the residents of my hometown. －－ Fighting "stone fights."

The so-called "stone fight" means that this kind of war does not use guns and artillery weapons, but completely uses stone blocks. The participants in the war are, of course, ordinary simple-minded and stubborn adults and youths. They live in the countryside, and the concept of family is very deep, living together as a family, and working together. If there is encroachment on their fields, or insults to their "own people," the solution is a battle. So they hold a "stone fight." They do not understand what "the sorrowful beauty" is, but "letters of challenge" must be exchanged. The place and date are agreed, and they are eager to give the other party a good beating.

Their battlefield is mostly on the top of the mountain, with both sides occupying half of the mountain, and each side arranging the proper places for attack and ambush. Each side uses large baskets to carry countless large and small stones, which are sharp and hard, causing people to shudder. And what is more interesting is that they also prepare a lot of "cooked tobacco," - a kind of cheap tobacco often smoked by friends in Guangdong, coarse tobacco leaves, strong in taste, temporarily rolled up in paper to smoke - prepared to apply to the head after it has been pierced by stones to stop the bleeding.

Stone fights are mostly held in autumn - perhaps to take advantage of the coolness?

When I was in the countryside, I was not allowed to watch the stone fights much, partly because I was young, and partly because the family rules were strict - my grandmother did not allow me to be infected with bad impressions. But in the last year, I was fifteen years old, and I secretly went with my classmates, walked a long way, and went to the mountain to watch. The situation was tense, and you couldn't help but cover your head to watch. Large and small stones flew back and forth like shuttles on the east and west sides of the mountain, and both sides shouted and killed, as if facing a great enemy. There were deaths and injuries from time to time. ｜——At that time, my heart was always uneasy.

However, I have been in Shanghai for nine years, and I don't know if "stone fights" have been banned or not? People in the south are bloody, and often use a battle to see who is superior, but it is also too barbaric.

A Scene of Swindling

— Drunken Fool

Thieves can be stupid thieves. But swindlers cannot be made without clever people. Because swindlers must have meticulous minds and clever means, in order to prevent people from seeing through their flaws, get into their traps, and swindle people's property. Therefore, the skills of swindlers are worthy of people's exclamations. It is a pity that cleverness is misused, "abandoning the right path and not following it," and ultimately becomes a degenerate person in society.

Tobacco and paper shops are the easiest to be cheated by swindlers. Like a few days ago, a tobacco and paper shop in Nanshi, this city, was cheated out of about sixty dollars by the method of peddling copper coins. Recently, a small tobacco and paper shop near the alley where I live was also visited by a swindler. Although the loss was not much, the swindler only used a small trick. Now I am writing it out, so that those who open tobacco and paper shops can see it and pay attention.

A well-dressed Mr. A stepped into the tobacco and paper shop and said to the person inside the counter: "I want to buy six dollars worth of ×× brand cigarettes." The boss accepted this big business and hurriedly packed the cigarettes and handed them to him. A then took out a wallet and was about to pay. Suddenly, he showed a surprised expression and said: "Oh, I don't have enough money here. I live at number ×× in this alley, surnamed ×. Because there is something going on at home tomorrow, I am buying so many cigarettes. I will write you a note with my address, and you send someone to deliver the goods and pay the money." The boss said: "Everyone is a neighbor. In that case, I will have someone go with you now." So he ordered an apprentice in his teens to take the cigarettes and follow him. He entered the alley, turned a corner, and arrived. A stepped into the gate of number ××, and suddenly said to the apprentice: "Give me this thing, and then go get two dollars worth of soap, hurry up and come back, and I will pay you together." The apprentice handed over the cigarettes, and even looked inside, seeing A naturally go in. He obeyed the order meticulously and returned to the shop to get a big bag of soap. When he arrived at the house, he could not see A. He shouted at the top of his lungs: "Hey, the soap is here." A woman's head stretched out from the window upstairs and replied: "Who wants soap, you sent it to the wrong place." The apprentice was stunned for a moment and explained the reason. The woman also said: "This is a respectable family, there is no such person." The apprentice then realized that he had been cheated and burst into tears. Later, the boss also came upon hearing the news, asked about the situation, and could do nothing. He just cursed angrily, "Met a damn cheat". The apprentice still took the soap and went back quietly!

A MODERN MISS'S DAY

— Bo Chen

When the first half of the day in the office comes to a halt, Miss C from a certain mansion just gets up, lazily, and wearily.

She walks gently to the wireless radio, tunes it to a foreign radio station, and immediately, a quiet and moving Western melody begins to play. She sits on the soft sofa, smoking a "cigarette," humming along with the song on the record.

Casually flipping open the newspaper, several seductive advertisements jump into her eyes: ×× Company's 1933 most "modern" clothing grand sale. Then, "A-Er" has the car ready, she jumps in, and the car rolls down the asphalt road.

Returning from ×× Company, Mr. Zhang is sitting in the reception room. Ah, she bravely embraces him, a deep and sweet kiss.

"I'm taking you to see 'Feng Qiu Huang' this afternoon, my darling must do me the honor."

"Ah::::"

Lunch is at three o'clock. She busies herself with a half-day beauty treatment. Happily, amidst the sounds of voices and rustling clothes, she steps into the cinema, whispering sweet nothings::: Her heart is filled with the joy of spring.

She walks out of the cinema with a light smile.

"Vienna," A-Er asked her, and after her reply, the car rolls down the asphalt road again. | Late at night.

When dawn is just breaking and the workers are going to work, Miss C from a certain mansion has just gone to sleep, lazily, and wearily.

FOURTH COMPANY COMMANDER OF THE NORTHEAST

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Sixteen: Aching Heart Still Sends Blessings, Hasty Military Affairs Secretly Shift Troops

Even though Ji Zhi was facing away from this Zhang San, he couldn't help but blush when he heard these words. He was silent for a moment, and then asked: You rickshaw pullers, whenever you stop at a place, you like to talk about the people who live there, are you just making things up? Zhang San was a little unconvinced when he heard this, so he stopped, turned his head, and looked at him, saying: Second Master, if you don't believe me, let's take a little detour, and walk along Haidian Street, if we're lucky, we'll see them walking down the street arm in arm. Ji Zhi suddenly replied: That's fine, so the two of them didn't say anything, the rickshaw pulled away quickly, heading towards Haidian Street. Ji Zhi sat in the rickshaw, seeing the Haidian market street getting closer and closer, he suddenly stomped his foot on the footrest several times and said: Don't pull forward, I'm not going to Haidian. Zhang San said: Now that we're here, there's no other way to go except through Haidian. As he said this, the rickshaw continued to pull forward as usual. Ji Zhi couldn't stop him, and he was too embarrassed to jump out of the rickshaw, so he sighed twice in the rickshaw. Zhang San was a little strange in his heart, taking him to Haidian was a very normal thing, why did he seem so unhappy. So he pulled the rickshaw for a while, and couldn't help but turn his head to look at Ji Zhi a couple of times. Ji Zhi was very afraid that he would see that he was jealous. So he smiled and said: If you want to take me to Haidian, then I'll let you take me. Zhang San laughed and said: Really, I'm not wronging you, they're very close, they often go to the milk tea shop hand in hand to talk. If you don't believe me, go to the milk tea shop and ask around. Ji Zhi smiled and said: Do I look like someone who likes to meddle in other people's business? Zhang San laughed, and pulled the rickshaw quickly to Haidian Street. Ji Zhi thought to himself, he had lived on Haidian Street before, so even if he took a rickshaw and passed through the street, it was a very normal thing, so why make things difficult for himself. So he kept a straight face and let Zhang San pull him along. (198)

World Oddities

THE CHINESE NATION IN THE EYES OF THE FRENCH

— Zhu Mei, from France

France is worthy of being called a civilized country because all its facilities are on track. Not many French people are well-educated, and they do not have the idea of harming others. They absolutely love their rights, but their love for obligations is exactly the same as their love for rights. It is not difficult to imagine what kind of people they would think the Chinese nation is with this kind of mindset. Especially what we give them from the facts, that is, the impression that the Chinese give them after coming to France and contacting them, and secondly, the influence that their education gives them. In Europe, France is considered to be better to the Chinese, although they do not like the Chinese very much, because almost all the people they approach are small vendors, carrying a small suitcase, unable to speak French, with yellow, dark, thin, and small faces, and untidy clothes. These Chinese not only live in Paris, but also scattered throughout all the cities and remote fields of France. And Chinese students with knowledge, they are of course difficult to approach, they are all studying in universities in big cities, and cannot run to small places for no reason. Therefore, as long as they have seen the Chinese, they always add many bad mocking adjectives when they talk about them. If they accidentally meet a clean and polite Chinese student, they often regard them as Japanese. Speaking of their education, French secondary education is the most corrupt for China. I have investigated their history and geography textbooks, and personally reviewed their maps, and found many surprising things. Their world history's description of China is entirely a century ago, with faces not only yellow, but also with a tail on their heads. Even more strange is that a woman's bound feet are specially placed on the table and photographed. Regarding this matter, I explained to the French people I knew, I said that this is already a historical relic. Didn't France also have many terrible bad habits in the past? However, they did see these kind of small-footed women in Paris in 1933. At that time, I thought those French people were spreading rumors, or maybe they were Chinese old ladies; later, after my investigation, there are not only many small-footed women in Paris, they are still peddlers, carrying a small baby on their backs, not only not old women but also very young. If such women are used to specify that all Chinese women are like this, isn't it too wronged? But in this way, they use historical events from more than a hundred years ago as textbooks, and now they still seem to think it is fresh. Secondly, speaking of geography, I think the French geography books are probably written by the Japanese themselves. How do you say that? That is, even with the old China, there are twenty-two provinces without any discount, but their descriptions of China only focus on the south, without mentioning how many provinces China has. So they ask me which province I am from? I said Sichuan, they can't understand that China has a Sichuan. And the map is even more absurd. No matter which country in the world, there is a special map. Even a small country like Japan has one equal to the size of England. China is only on a map of Asia, and the entire China only has four provinces: Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Yunnan, and Guangdong. The remaining provinces, such as Sichuan and Hunan, are absolutely not there. There is a Tibet province, and the color of Tibet province is exactly the same as the color of England and the British colonies, and the color of Manchuria is the same as Japan. At that time, I asked a friend who was a geography teacher in a middle school, is that map recently published? He said it has been more than twenty years. In addition, I also saw a world map, each country distinguished by color, and at the same time, each country used a person to describe the unique spirit of that country. For example, the United States is a very well-dressed gentleman, holding a bookkeeping book in his hand, indicating that this is a country that manages commerce, Germany, England, Poland, Russia, Japan, etc.::: everything that should be there, and the Japanese are barefoot and hard-working, but there is no China on the entire world map! This is a world map, and it is a textbook for all low-level schools in France. Let us think, what is the impression of the Chinese nation that the French are cultivated from such education?

FLUCTUATIONS IN THE SECURITIES AND PUBLIC BOND MARKET

The situation in North China is serious... Many [sellers] flocked to market.

Military cuts fell 2.6 yuan... Much like a limit down situation.

Trading was extremely lively... Future prospects are still cloudy.

Yesterday, the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange experienced huge changes in various bond markets. The situation in North China became increasingly serious, and the market was timely at the last day of the September futures, and the bulls panicked greatly. The long position of a certain silver company of two to three million surged into the market. The initial situation at the opening of the morning market was extremely bad, and there was a limit down situation. Because the military cuts fell by 1.5 yuan, the military cuts fell sharply by 2.65 yuan this month due to the frantic selling on the 21st. Long-dated futures were immediately bought in, so the market price of long-dated futures exceeded that of the near-dated ones. This abnormal situation was completely forced by the short squeeze. Thereafter, the situation gradually entered a normal path, but the decline did not diminish, and gradually became peaceful, with limited falls, such as only a small four-jiao decrease in long-dated salt tax. This kind of wave, one is that the September futures were only on this day, one is that the environment was unfavorable to the long position, and even more because it had been brewing for more than a month, once it fell sharply, it would also be fierce. Trading was extremely active, and the second session was not opened until 2 p.m. The market price was relatively stable due to some of the short positions taking advantage of the situation, but it was still mixed and chaotic, with highs and lows alternating, and people's hearts were extremely flustered. The afternoon opening did not take place until 5 p.m., but the shorts had a lot of offsetting, the trading surged, and the prices returned to 35 jiao or so, depending on the stock. The closing was approaching 9 p.m., the market was still a short squeeze, near soft and far strong, and the prices were slightly better by 34 jiao. As a result, those whose market prices fell, such as military cuts, and those who did poorly lost five jiao to over one and a half yuan, and also fell more and rose less. The long-dated unified salt tax and gold shorts all rose well, by two or three jiao to over four jiao. Today there is only one month of October futures, and its volatility will be no small matter, and the price may not be able to return to strength immediately. The future prospects are still cloudy. The total volume traded was approximately 25 million or so.

Free Talk

August in Hangzhou

— Yu Dafu

August in the lunar calendar in Hangzhou is also a very lively month. Starting from the fifteenth day of the seventh month, osmanthus and chestnuts are on the market. Entering August, there are even more chestnuts, and the osmanthus flowers in the Manjuelong, Nan Gaofeng, and Wengjiashan areas are even more fragrant and intoxicating. The name "Osmanthus Month" for August can only be truly understood after personally visiting Manjuelong.

In addition to the osmanthus flowers in August and the Mid-Autumn Festival on the fifteenth day of the eighth month, which is common in China, Hangzhou also has the Qiantang River tide on the eighteenth day of the eighth month.

The autumn tide of the Qiantang River has been famous for a long time. Legend has it that it is because King Fucha of Wu killed Wu Zixu and sank him in the river. Wu Zixu was dissatisfied, and his ghost was causing trouble. There is a passage in Lunheng that refutes this matter, and it is said with good reason: "The Confucian book says, 'King Fucha of Wu killed Wu Zixu, cooked him in a cauldron, put him in a bag, and threw him into the river. Wu Zixu was angry and made waves by the water, drowning people.' The statement that King Wu killed Wu Zixu and threw him into the river is true, but the statement that he was resentful and made waves by the water is false. Moreover, Wei chopped Zilu, and Han cooked Peng Yue. Wu Zixu was brave, but no more than Zilu and Peng Yue, but the two men could not become angry in the cauldron. Wu Zixu was also the same. He first entered the cauldron and then entered the river. Why was his spirit timid in the cauldron and brave in the river? Why is his anger inconsistent before and after?" However, although the reasoning of Lunheng is sufficient, the power of legend is ultimately very great. To this day, not only at the head of the Qiantang River, but also on the banks of the Fei River in Luzhou City and in coastal areas around lakes in Jiangsu and Fujian, one can still see the temple of Grand Master Wu with a white horse and a plain carriage.

The tide of the Qiantang River must have been even larger in ancient times than it is now. This can be understood from the fact that the eminent monk Shi Baoda of Lingyin Temple in the Tang Dynasty recited spells to prevent the river tide from hitting the mountains on the lake, and that Emperor Gaozong of the Southern Song Dynasty watched the tide only at the Gao Tai of the pagoda outside the Hou Chao Gate in Jianggan. Now, one must go east to Haining or Wubao or Babao to see the line of silver sea tide crest. This can also be seen in Ruan Yuan's Yan Jing Shi Ji Zhejiang Tu Kao, and the sand swelling in the river is the biggest reason why the tide does not come far.

Also, in the fourth year of the Kai Ping era of the Liang Dynasty, King Qian Musu of Wu built a sea embankment and ordered hundreds of strong crossbows to shoot at the tide head, only outside the Hou Chao Tongjiang Gate. To this day, the iron cow town castings along the Haining River are clearly the relics of King Wusu, things made by later generations. (I remember the year of the iron cow casting was in the Shunzhi era of the Qing Dynasty, and the words printed on the cow's body were still faintly discernible.)

The changes in the world are truly terrible, but even now, there are still quite a few residents of Hangzhou who make a small fortune by relying on this autumn tide and doing this business!

The Dream of the Literary Canon

— Da Yi

I have already published an article entitled "The Dream of the Taoist Canon" in Free Talk. Someone asked, "It is already the case that the characters in The Scholars are good at arguing over the Taoist canon: do you have anything to say about the characters in The Writers also arguing over the literary canon?" I said, "Those who argue over the literary canon have been favored by the ancient prose writers since the Tang and Song dynasties. By the time of the Qing Dynasty, parallel prose revived, and the likes of Ruan Yuan and Wang Zhong almost won the orthodox position for parallel prose. If one speaks of its origin, the Taoist canon is the same source as the literary canon. The Sage Confucius bears two shoulders, one shoulder of the Taoist canon and one shoulder of the literary canon. When the Tao is not lost, the culture is not lost. It is tied to one person, the so-called since the birth of the people, there has never been someone like my Master."

The dream of the literary canon has always been held by the writers of the Southern and Northern Dynasties. Liu Xie wrote The Literary Mind and the Carving of Dragons, and its preface roughly says: "When I was over thirty, I once dreamed at night of holding a ceremonial vessel painted with red lacquer and following Confucius south. When I awoke, I was happy and said, 'Great is the difficulty of seeing a sage. Could it be a dream bestowed on me, a small child?' To praise the sacred will, nothing is better than annotating the classics, but the scholars of Ma Zheng have already elaborated on them with precision, and even with profound interpretations, it is not enough to establish a school. Only the use of literature is actually the technique of the classics. The five rites rely on it to be completed, and the six codes use it to be effective." Therefore, I picked up a pen and mixed ink, and then began to write about literature. It can be seen that Liu Xie dreamed of Confucius and implicitly shouldered the literary canon himself, while letting the Taoist canon go to the pedantic scholars of the classics. It is a pity that he attacked heterodoxy and converted to Buddhism, which is the same disease as those who vainly shoulder the Taoist canon today, bringing shame to the past sages without knowing it.

Jiang Yan was famous for his writing when he was young, but his talent and thoughts declined slightly in his later years. He once dreamed at night that Zhang Jingyang said to him, "I sent you a bolt of brocade before, now you can return it to me." Jiang Yan searched in his arms and got a few feet to give to him. Zhang was greatly angered and said, "How can you cut it all up!" He also dreamed of seeing Guo Pu, who said, "I have a pen in your place for many years, you can return it to me." Jiang Yan searched in his arms and got a five-colored law to give to him. Jiang Lang only said that he dreamed of inheriting the traditions of the Jin poets Zhang Jingyang and Guo Pu, and dared not remotely inherit the literary canon of the Sage Confucius. Could it be that he was exhausted in his later years that he was willing to make this particularly self-denying statement?

When Ji Shaoyu was young, he once dreamed that Lu Chui gave him a bundle of blue carved brushes and said, "I can still use this pen. You choose the best one for yourself." His writing became more powerful because of this. When Zheng Zhuo was young, he once dreamed of meeting Huang Kan on the road. Kan said, "Zheng Lang, open your mouth." Kan then spat into Zheng Zhuo's mouth, and his understanding of principles improved. Li Guang extensively read books and had talent and thought, comparable to Xing and Wei. He once wanted to go to court early, took a nap, and suddenly woke up, saying to his wife, "I seemed to be sleeping but not sleeping just now. Suddenly I saw a person come out of my body and say, 'You are working too hard, and your spirit cannot bear it. Now I am leaving you.'" He was dazed and unhappy because of this, and fell ill after a few days and never recovered. Dreaming of the poetic soul leaving the body and the poet dying, dreaming of the literary giants giving pens and the literary thoughts advancing, dreaming of the philosophers giving saliva and the principles becoming refined - why did the literati of this era often have strange dreams, and could dreams actually be verified? In those days, writers were fond of boasting, and the habit was deeply rooted. Entrusting dreams to show differences was one of their techniques for exaggerating that they were inheriting the literary canon of the ancients or their predecessors. Even writers who were not worth mentioning would also engage in vain exaggeration: Wu Maiyuan liked to elevate himself and despise others. Whenever he wrote a poem and got a satisfying phrase, he would throw it to the ground and shout, "What is Cao Zijian worth mentioning!" Shan Chao heard and laughed, saying, "In the past, Liu Jixu's talent was not as good as the author, but he liked to criticize people's articles. Jixu is trivial, how can he be worth talking about!" As for Maiyuan, what is he doing? Also, Yuan Gu of Chen County valued his writing and said to people, "My poems should be blocked by great talents, otherwise they will fly away." These kinds of arrogant people can hardly be explained except by what modern psychologists call megalomania.

Travel Notes (Continued)

— Tianma

"Bring his baggage in! An umbrella and a quilt are also okay!" The accountant ordered again.

Then the crying started, begging the master for mercy, and floating above the crying and begging sounds were scoldings, insults, and the cries of pain from being hit. It was all mixed together.

Every time I encountered such a tragedy, I couldn't bear to watch it, but I couldn't bear not to watch it. This tragedy is precisely a symbol of rural bankruptcy.

The poor farmers came to the city with golden dreams, and then returned to the countryside with the sadness of disappointment. They were wandering and displaced.

Three Lonely Hills

The boat passed Lonely Hill, just at a beautiful sunset, the setting sun sinking into the water, the colors of the clouds changing, the scenery like a painting. Standing on the highest deck of the boat, I saw from afar that verdant spot, as if it were going to flow eastward with the water in the surging river. The closer the boat got, the more Lonely Hill stood tall and upright in the heart of the river, its feet standing as firm as iron, scornfully glaring at the turbid flow under its feet. The surging and roaring river water rushed head-on, but when it reached its feet, it could only helplessly drag the sighs of defeat and escape past its side.

Seeing Lonely Hill, I thought of Jun Mountain in my hometown again. But Jun Mountain is bigger than Lonely Hill, and the lake water is not as turbulent as the river flow. We certainly don't have to worry that it will be swept away by the stormy waves one day. As for Lonely Hill, it is only the size of a green snail, and it is standing in the turbulent river, but it seems to be more stable and serious than Mount Tai. No matter the wind and rain, no matter the angry tide that overwhelms the sky and the sea, it cannot shake its feet. This really makes me sincerely feel respect.

Mr. Tao Xingzhi once had a poem about Lonely Hill:

"Who says Lonely Hill is small? Its feet are firmly planted; it commands the waters of the Yangtze River, winding around it on both sides." Another poem is:

"Who says Lonely Hill is small? Lonely Hill is old; East and West going ships, how much do they know about floating and sinking?"

Of the two poems, I like the phrase "feet firmly planted" the most. I feel that only that sentence is the most powerful, the most touching, and only that sentence is truly worthy of praising Lonely Hill.

In a Third-Class Carriage

— Ba Jin

－One of the Travel Essays

Sitting on a train doesn't seem like a pleasant thing, and a third-class carriage is certainly not a comfortable place, but I have spent part of my time in a third-class carriage in the past year or two. It seems that some people have said that they envy the life I live. They would not know these situations.

I had been saying I was going to leave for a week or two. Some friends would meet me on the road and ask, "Why are you still in Shanghai?" I couldn't find a second sentence except for the short reply, "I'm leaving tomorrow." Indeed, I was preparing to "leave tomorrow" every day, but unexpectedly, this "tomorrow" dragged on for a week or two. The injustice is that some people suspected that I was deliberately deceiving them.

One evening, after seeing Mr. and Mrs. W off on the train, I walked to the China Travel Service with M. Neither of us was familiar with the roads in Shanghai. At that time, I had not decided to leave that night, nor had I decided to go to the China Travel Service to buy tickets. We were just walking on those relatively flat roads, talking about the problems that had been tormenting our young hearts for so long. We could not see the surrounding scenery. M and I, like each other, had a picture of the future engraved in our hearts. We believed that this picture showed a stage that human society must go through in the process of evolution. However, others did not acknowledge it. They said we were deceiving ourselves with fantasies. We did not feel that we were wrong. The picture could not be washed away. When it was first engraved in our hearts, it had taken a lot of the craftsman's effort and a long time. For us, it would always be a source of inspiration, constantly bringing us hope, especially after our friend X brought good news from a distant Mediterranean ancient country a few days ago. Although M and I were both filled with emotions of parting, we did not feel sad. Our conversation at that time was all about the future, and those were beautiful words.

The sky gradually darkened, but we didn't notice it; the lights came on, and we didn't notice it either. The bright and beautiful prospects loomed vaguely before our eyes. Unintentionally, we walked to the China Travel Service on Sichuan Road, and we went in to buy tickets.

"When are you leaving?"

"Tonight."

I answered without hesitation. When I got out the door, I realized: I'm leaving tonight. At this moment, I suddenly felt how unfortunate it was to waste time on trains and ships.

×××

The luggage was packed temporarily, which didn't take much time. When Mr. and Mrs. V saw me off at the station, it was only a little after ten o'clock, and the train was not scheduled to depart until twelve o'clock. I didn't need anyone to see me off at the station, but Mrs. V said, "Walking alone is lonely, and it's pitiful not to have anyone to see you off." I couldn't refuse them either.

On the platform, we found M. He was waiting for us there. Now no one would feel lonely anymore. V was carrying my rattan bag, and we got on the train.

There were few passengers in the carriage, and there were many empty seats. I took out the bedding from the rattan bag and spread it on the long bench, thinking that I would definitely be able to sleep comfortably tonight. (To be continued)

文盲撲滅所（四）

— 康司坦丁·斐爾作林翼之譯

"But you say the iron smelter factory has nothing to do with you, then you are mistaken, this is definitely not unrelated to you."

"I don't know," Maria Fortovna said timidly, and then asked: "Do you know everything that is written in the newspaper?"

"Is there anything I don't know," Dingjia said with a wry smile: "Of course, I know everything."

"Do you hope to start work on May 15th?"

Dingjia smiled:

"Of course, I hope so." After a moment of silence, he said firmly: "The whole country hopes so, so I hope so, and you..."

Like this······"

"What, me?" she said in surprise.

"Of course, you also hope so." Dingjia said decisively: "Of course, you also hope so, aren't you an intellectual worker who is advancing with us, how can we not understand this?"

"But I don't quite understand." she said.

"Maybe that's how it will be," Dingjia agreed: "This kind of thing often happens, I myself didn't understand it in the past. I am sixty years old this year, but I have only just understood it now. I am sixty years old, but you are probably not even forty years old."

"I'm thirty-seven," she said, blushing.

"That's right, it must be because of age, although I am sixty this year, I am not old yet." His expression was unusually serious, as if he was talking about a great principle.

"What kind of person do you think I am?" he asked solemnly.

"I don't know."

"I am a degenerate, a rogue class."

"What?" Maria Fortovna never expected that Dingjia, who looked like a farmer, would say such a thing, and was really taken aback.

"A rogue class." Dingjia repeated.

"A wandering drunkard, but now, I am a member of the shock troops, a proletariat, I have only walked a single path in my life,"

"But now, it has turned into two feet, and every step is firmly on the ground, surrounded by factories and construction projects."

He said goodbye to Maria and strode off to the opposite side. (The End)

Informal Essay

On Hope by You Yi

People nowadays say; "Let us not grieve over the past, nor should we yearn for the future, we must grasp the present, the present."

What is called "yearning for the future" is "hope."

"Hope" for people can sometimes ignite an upward passion, but sometimes it can also lead to discouragement due to disappointment.

"Hope" originally has no limit, and the goal is not easy to achieve.

In fact, "hope" is ultimately inseparable from people, for example, my "hope" when writing this piece is that I can write it more substantively, like an actor performing on stage, and be able to win a little more applause. And when this piece is written and sent to the newspaper office, I hope it will be published sooner.

However, "hope" is, after all, mostly elusive. When I was in elementary school, at about ten years old, our Chinese teacher gave us a composition topic called "My Ambition," so many innocent elementary school students used their simple brains, stretching out paper and sucking on brushes, with undivided attention. Some said they wanted to be great politicians like Zhuge Liang: some said they wanted to be great inventors like Watt: some also said they wanted to be invincible generals like Sun Tzu, and some wanted to be great industrialists, and some wanted to develop mineral resources. At that time, didn't I also take it upon myself to help the world and the people, and my ambition was unmatched? But for more than ten years, I have been running around and experienced what is called "worldliness," and although my lofty aspirations have not completely faded, I have no longer the dreams of those years.

But "hope" still exists after all. The reason why I can still drag my wounded body and struggle on the road of life is because "hope" is encouraging me and urging me from behind; I not only "hope" but also believe that I think there is still hope for China now. At the same time, I believe even more that the light will eventually come.

Of course, "hope" is a bit close to self-deception, but rational hope is right. And achieving the "goal" is also easier.

When I work, I grasp the reality, but I am not just working hard in silence, I am also looking to the "future" on the one hand, I am looking at how much road is left to my "hope"? And sometimes I also look back at the "past," but I am not "grieving," but "reviewing the old to learn the new."

However, the "hope" on the other hand is a bit unflattering, just like the ticket price of the ×× lottery is one yuan, and the first prize is indeed 50,000 yuan, who would not want to spend an old silver dollar to try their luck, and if they hit it, it would be 50,000 times the interest, and they would immediately rise to the top and become a wealthy man, what a lucky thing! However, however, after all, only one person out of 500,000 people hits this so-called "luck," and 499,999 people will be disappointed!

After all, "hope" is mostly elusive.

However, when "realistic goals" are used to replace "rational hope," then it is indispensable.

The Relationship Between "Production" and "Consumption" by Er Chu

Often, we know very well that the evolution of society is based on mankind's continuous "production" and continuous "consumption." Because consumption seeks to satisfy the universal desires of mankind, - and the desires of mankind increase with the needs of the times - the so-called universal desires are the essential elements of life, such as clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Mankind has been busy with "production" morning and night, without rest, all for the sake of "consumption." In other words, it is to satisfy one's own desires. Then, there should be no objection to the saying "production" for "consumption," right?

Desires that are above the waterline are extravagant hopes.

To "consume" in order to satisfy a certain extravagant hope, that should be called "waste."

China is a country with backward "production," this should be an undeniable fact, right? Chinese people, except for the only farmers - and now the countryside has collapsed, what else can be said - work hard from early morning to dark, year after year "producing," most of the others only know how to "consume" - even waste, especially the general masters, gentlemen, wives, and young ladies in the city, they, they are doing the so-called "higher Chinese" under the command of foreigners, what do these "slaves of the masters" know about "production," maybe they do know, can "produce," that is to "produce" for foreigners, living in foreign houses, riding in motorcycles, promoting foreign goods,··· almost not even eating Chinese rice, but eating foreign bread. - In fact, there are many - alas! Rural collapse, backward production!

Therefore, the abnormal phenomenon of "consumption" exceeding "production" is bound to appear. Foreign goods take the opportunity to flood the market, forming what is now called China as an "international market"! It is very heartbreaking to say!

The exhibition of this phenomenon is caused by the mutual surpassing of "production" and "consumption." Because "production" dominates "consumption," "consumption" dominates desire, and desire dominates "production." If a certain transcendence or lag breaks the interrelated cycle, a considerable horror is bound to be revealed. This kind of horror is the social unrest and the instability of personal life. If "production" surpasses "consumption," of course, there will be worries about overproduction. (The current European and American countries are in this situation.) "Consumption" surpasses "production," and it affects economic panic. Our China is properly shouting and clamoring about the chaos of backward "production" and economic panic, which constitutes social unrest and the instability of personal life, only being tempted by the "consumption" of Europe and the United States, and eagerly seeking to imitate. Thus, it automatically alienated the "national concept" and the "path of self-salvation," and all consumption tends to be Europeanized, "producing" for foreigners and promoting foreign goods, rescuing overproduced Europe and the United States. However, the "production" of Europe and the United States is put aside, and it is still in the intersection of the 18th century handicraft industry and the 19th century iron industry, far from the "production" of Europe and the United States!

In short, "production" and "consumption" must have equal development in order to gradually seek progress. This geometric rule, in any case, tells us like the "ㄧ." Who dares to deny it?

Page 21

A Person in a Stormy Night by Jian Ping

It was a stormy night. Pearl-like raindrops were pouring down rapidly and intensively; the roaring wind almost lifted the umbrella-holding pedestrians into the air! At ten o'clock, I went to the No. 9 bus station on Avenue Foch, and waited until half past ten without seeing the shadow of the bus. I thought it must be because of the storm, and there would be no more buses running! So I changed direction and ran to Route Westmore to take the tram.

I got on the No. 1 tram, and the car was full of wet drops, and my clothes were all soaked, and I felt strangely cold and shivering. Looking out of the car window through the glass covered with sweat, not only were there no pedestrians, but even all kinds of vehicles were as rare as morning stars. In fact, it was only ten forty-five at this time, which should be the lively time in the city. There were several people in yellow uniforms in the car, probably employees of the tram company, who were saying, "There are two more No. 7 trams." This should be a great comfort to me, because I need the No. 7 tram to take me home.

Got off the bus at the Bund. The wind was even stronger, and the rain poured down on the earth like a torrent of water - although I had a small umbrella in my hand, it had lost its effect, and the handle had been broken by the wind - the cold rain soaked my whole body, and soon a car full of drowned chickens came, and I desperately squeezed into the car, seeming to have found a shelter, and suddenly felt the joy of finding a way out. At this time, the river water was pouring onto the shore, and the road had become small rivers, and the four- or five-inch-high street edges were submerged in the flowing water! On the road! It shouldn't be said that in the center of the small river, cars were driving past one by one, and they couldn't be as crazy and mighty as usual. Its half-submerged wheels were driving in the water, like the action of a motorboat.

Our tram was hesitating at the intersection of Broadway Road and Seward Road. The passengers meant to go to Seward Road, because Broadway Road was low-lying, and it was expected that the water would be very deep. But the driver, without stating the reason, said, "The foreign foreman has ordered to go to Broadway Road." So he braved the rain to get out of the car and chisel the road, chiseling for a full fifteen minutes. We really couldn't wait any longer, and on the one hand, we saw the water on the road gradually rising. As a result, we still took Seward Road, and we didn't verify the words of his foreign foreman "there is unexpected danger." At half past eleven, I arrived home safely.

Now! It is when I pick up my pen to write this news, the wind has stopped, the rain has stopped, the small river has been restored to a road, my wet clothes have dried; the lovely sun in the sky has also proudly displayed its great "power" ······ Everything is no different from usual, only our body and mind feel very comfortable and relaxed - therefore, I got an inspiration:

When the weather reaches a certain time, there will inevitably be an amazing storm. But one thing, we should understand that in the process of this storm, undoubtedly, every passerby will encounter considerable difficulties. At this time, we need not be alarmed, not escape, but endure and struggle! Because, in the near future, it will be our comfort and relaxation, the sunny day when the sun re-displays its great "power" proudly!

Where is Your Home? By Jian Ping

It was about five o'clock in the afternoon on the Saturday before last! The Zhenhu train, which I was sitting on from the pier, finally parked weakly at Zhenru Station. I was just trying to tidy up the books and newspapers that had been turned upside down on this long journey, so as not to imprison my tired body again when I arrived in Shanghai.

Suddenly, a chaotic sound of leather shoes and the English sound of "incarnate evil" broke the temporary silence in the carriage. I turned around and saw two wealthy customers of our Chinese future - college students - coming up, so I couldn't help but pay attention to them, but they simply didn't see a poor writer like me.

The car moved slowly again, and a carload of passengers stretched lazily in unison, which was naturally a quick indication that the destination was about to arrive; but the two college students, like fresh troops, were talking endlessly in their English, what "Churchill Sten," and what "Smith Smith" simply didn't stop talking. Of course, most of the passengers in the third-class car were from the business community, so they couldn't help but admire and worship this pair of outstanding college students, so they became even more proud.

"May I ask you two gentlemen! Where is your home?" Suddenly, an old man in cloth, like Cheng Yaojin who was killed halfway, asked them kindly:

"Well! Guangdong Xiangshan, we are from the same hometown," they couldn't help but answer him with some suspicion:

"Guangdong Xiangshan seems to be still within our country's territory, why do you two speak foreign languages?" the old man asked further:

"This ······" The college students hesitated for a long time, but still didn't answer. It just so happened that the car had arrived at the station at this time, which invisibly relieved their embarrassment.

Spare Time Mailbox

Not Enough Strength

Editor:

I am a poor young man under the age of twenty, and I am now a small employee in a small shop; my income is very meager, and very pitiful. My family is also extremely burdened by the economy; I have received letters asking me to send money back. But I have no ability, so I want to find a more noble occupation. But I have more than enough heart but not enough strength, so I sit in a city of sorrow every day, and I am oppressed by this vicious environment. I am really at a loss. May I ask what I should do with such an environment? Please give me a satisfactory answer in your publication. Thank you very much. Sincerely,

Respectfully, Gu Yaohua

Editor's note: Mr. Gu wants to find a more noble position in order to take care of his poor family; this is the common wish of people in the current society. "People want high mountains and water want low, " who doesn't want to earn more money to serve their parents and support their wives? However, Mr. Gu didn't think about it any further. Why do you "not have enough strength"? How can you remedy "not enough strength"? Then you will know that you must work harder to cultivate yourself. Knowledge, experience, and worldliness are all necessary for cultivation. If, because you want to provide for a poor family, you only know that you want to find a more noble position: this is a mirage, and you will never get your wish in your life. You must think further about how to cultivate yourself. Although this kind of success cannot be expected overnight, it will naturally reach the goal one day in the long run. I hope that those in the world who "do not have enough strength" will rise up and catch up and cultivate their strength; do not engage in the business of "blaming God and complaining about others" or "drawing cakes to satisfy hunger," this is feasible. We have received many letters, and although what they say is different, they all only hope for an increase in income, and cannot take into account the cultivation of ability. This kind of thinking of abandoning the root and pursuing the branch, or it is one of the important reasons for the current state of unrest in society. I will take advantage of Mr. Gu's inquiry to elaborate as above.

Here, the editor has one more word to tell the world for the sake of parents. People originally have the obligation to educate their children, but now because of their own economic difficulties, they cannot fully fulfill this obligation, which is a regrettable thing that cannot be avoided; but at least to the limit, before they "do not have enough strength," they must not blame them too severely. I often see many promising young people, because their parents supervise them too strictly, and thus flow into the path of recklessness and luck, or even resort to cheating, and finally their ambition is completely dispelled, which is really a pity. There are no parents in the world who do not love their children, please pay attention.

War and Peace (34) (Four-Act Play) Ling He

Act III Praise of Peace

Principal: Humph, isn't it? So now our only avenue is to resist desperately. We should resist for self-defense, we should fight for righteousness. (At this time, the military authorities have already reached the stairs.) As long as we continue to resist, the final victory will belong to the side of justice.

Confidential Secretary: That's right, what you said is the meaning of the government's long-term resistance. The current ceasefire is also a further step in long-term resistance.

Principal: (Seeing the military authorities stand up.) Sorry, I have delayed your official duties.

Military Authorities: It's nothing, please sit down. What's the matter?

Principal: It's about the ceasefire, I want to ask for advice. Recently, the general students are very resentful about this ceasefire. They say that such direct negotiations are too weak. They are all young people and do not understand the general situation of the country, and they always blame the government everywhere. So I want to know some important meanings about the ceasefire here, so that I can go back and enlighten them.

Military Authorities: Regarding the significance of this ceasefire, I think every Chinese citizen should understand; China is now so poor and exhausted, can it still withstand years of war? This is the first point. Second, the communists are rampant in Jiangxi, Hunan, and other places, disturbing the country, which is simply a hidden danger for the government, so we weigh the importance, and we must first settle the internal before we can resist the external. Third, China's weapons and equipment are too backward, which is very important. Can the broadsword team block airplanes and artillery? You don't know the situation on the battlefield, it is said that the tanks rolled over like a landslide, and our position was completely lost. The fourth point, I guess you know even if I don't say it. That is to say, our combat power cannot be balanced. Because they all want to preserve their strength. For example, last month the enemy was about to attack Nantianmen, and our army detected it in advance, so it specifically ordered a certain unit to attack Guyuan, towards the Luanping Avenue, to attack the enemy's right wing, but who knew that the commander of that unit disobeyed the order, made excuses and did not advance, and later Nantianmen, fought day and night, and sacrificed a mess. Not only that, some infantry teams are simply using the name of resisting Japan to actually expand their military strength. For example, a certain unit of the Northwest Army, without obeying the central government's order, knew how to move and came from southern Jin. What is the intention of this? Everyone knows that it is to seize territory. Since they have come, then the central government has always been generous, and of course it is not convenient to stop them. Now stationed in Dingzhou, claiming to be two divisions, but in fact there are only more than 4,000 people and more than 2,800 miscellaneous guns. So we reorganized and supplemented him, and ordered him to go to Luandong to participate in the war. But they took this opportunity to threaten military pay. Originally, when the reorganization was done, it was only said that the monthly pay was 33,000, but later they said that it would be 160,000 yuan a month, otherwise they would stay put. Look, in this situation, how embarrassed are our central troops? Is it difficult for us to be all fools? If the enemy knows about this kind of thing, they will really laugh until their stomachs hurt.

Principal: Yes, how many common people are angered to death by this situation.

Military Authorities: So, we can't stop the war for the sake of the common people. These grievances, please ask the gentleman to tell the people of the country.

Film Special Issue

Colleen Moore's Return to the Silver Screen

— by Her

The Number One Star of the Silent Era

Seeking Work Again After Four Years of Wandering

Colleen Moore's name, I guess it's not easy for us to forget. Although she has been away from the film industry for several years, we still feel very excited when we hear her name. She is not only the most popular star of the silent era, but what especially ties her to the hearts of Chinese people is that her oval face, matched with dark and shiny hair, cut straight across the eyebrows, is like a fashionable little Chinese girl, so Chinese audiences are of course not a few who are infatuated with her.

In the silent era, Colleen Moore was the highest-paid star. When she retired from the film industry in 1929, she had accumulated millions of fortunes. Some people say it was more than one million, as many as three million. At that time, she was only twenty-seven years old. Because she was rich, she wanted to enjoy a free life for a while, so she wandered around for four years. In these four years, she tried all kinds of ways to spend her time and seek other ways to express her talent besides movies. She hired famous teachers to study oil painting and sculpture. Without success, she went to study music. Because she had studied piano before entering the film industry, she thought she would definitely succeed this time. But in the end, she still couldn't calm her heart. As a result, she understood that besides movies, she had no other way out; besides work, there was no other way to find happiness. So she resolutely returned to Hollywood. This was last year.

MGM heard that Colleen Moore was back and signed a long-term contract with her. But for a year, no matter how many scripts were discussed, none were suitable for her status, so there was no work for a long time. Although MGM was cautious in handling things, it had to be so, but Colleen Moore came with a stomach full of enthusiasm, and what she needed was work, not money, so a year of idleness caused her great mental pain. Fortunately, Fox Company later saw that she had nothing to do and borrowed her to perform in a play called The Power and the Glory o. Since this film was successful, Hollywood has known that Colleen Moore's acting talent has not regressed because of four years of leisure; secondly, she is now a woman over thirty, her works have changed, and she is very suitable for playing the role of middle-aged women.

Colleen Moore's acting talent is beyond doubt. That kind of light and lively posture and delicate and appropriate expression can be said to be superb in the silent era. Unfortunately, she, like Manly Bickford, Li Ling Jishu, etc., suffered the sudden blow of the voice film invasion, which made her have to take a vacation herself. Anyone who has seen her films such as Lilac Time and Orchids and Ermine will feel endless regret for her. Just looking at her performing expression is so delicate, but how disappointing it is when she opens her mouth to sing. Of course, in the early days of sound films, there were many defects in all sound recording techniques. Now everything has improved, and it can make up for this defect in pronunciation. However, we also thought that the little girl with dark and shiny hair and a round face is no longer visible; the changes in four years make people feel a lot of vicissitudes!

Film Review

Review of "Her First Mate"

— Bai

— Cathay Film —

If we definitively acknowledge that movies are one of the tools for educating the public, then in my personal opinion, the performance of this film not only fails to adequately fulfill its mission, but is also wasteful.

In fact, the American and European film industries are truly nearing the eve of decline. Due to a lack of scripts, they are piecing together material from various sources, only to use topics that cater to the base desires of some people. They either use women's "sex appeal" to numb and deceive, or rely on slapstick comedy or thrilling adventures to elicit a brief laugh from the audience. This film, "Her First Mate," undoubtedly arose from this chaotic and poorly produced state, even though it is not as dazzling as usual!

Here! We must first explain the content of the story. It depicts John Honor, the son of a seafarer, who is forced by circumstances to not inherit his father's profession. Therefore, he goes through many hardships and later gets assistance from his wife to become the owner of a ferry. The screenwriter's main purpose is clearly to depict the true love of a couple sharing their lives, so the story ends in a comedic way. However, anyway, I think this point is precisely where the play's mistake lies. We must know that in this society, there are many people who behave like the protagonist in the story. It is inappropriate for the screenwriter not to strictly correct this, but to give it a gratifying praise. From what John Honor tells us on screen, although the screenwriter wants to portray him as a person with ambitious thoughts, in reality, he is just a complete mediocrity. To boast to his wife, he deceitfully claims to be a first mate. He wants to buy a sailboat, but insists on using his wife's money. Doesn't this clearly show us what a useless man is? And the result is these scenes. I think this kind of concept is really unacceptable - at least it will not make a good contribution to society.

In terms of performance, there is not much achievement. The director's skills are mediocre. However, as mentioned earlier, this play is not as dazzling as usual, but uses a humorous method to perform, which should be commendable. The actors are very faithful. The female lead Zasu Pitts can be said to be successful. The rest have very little room for development under the control of this kind of plot.

So, apart from the selection of material, which is somewhat realistic, this film is generally very ordinary.

Audience opinions

Yesterday's Flowers: Review of "The Light of Motherhood"

— Mo Naihe

Although "The Light of Motherhood" is already yesterday's flowers, it still has value for review. Because of the high artistic value of the work, I do not mind the details, and write some opinions.

In general, this is a valuable work. Because the writer admires the work too much, therefore, he finds two points to offer:

The first point is that when Jiahuan returns from Nanyang and meets his ex-wife Huiying, calling her "Mrs. Lin" seems to have a bit of a sour taste. A person who has been whipped in front and behind by the mine owner, and at the same time understands a little more about this society, and who has done practical revolutionary work before, should not have this sour taste. When Jiahuan called her "Mrs. Lin," some of the audience made mocking laughter, which damaged the "light" of this mother.

Another point: when the mother is grieving, the sudden appearance of the three comedic stars caused the audience to roar with laughter when they saw their comedy. This point distracted the audience's emotions that were being organized.

Finally, when Huiying and Jiahuan are seen walking outside by Xiaomei, and Xiaomei and Shulin are in the midst of passion and excitement and are called away by their mother to be rebuked, she says, "Why is mother going out with Mr. Zou?" A group of audience laughed, thinking that this sentence was well said. I feel that our Chinese cultural level is still very low, and therefore I feel that movies are so important in this era, and should bear the responsibility of promoting the cultural level of the masses.

That's what I felt, so I scribbled it down.

Marlene's Lonely Residence

— Bing

When Marlene Dietrich first ran from Germany to California, the Hollywood newspapers published Marlene's address and published photos of the houses in her home. Since then, her home has often been visited by uninvited guests, because Marlene Dietrich is inherently hospitable, and she welcomes and entertains all visitors, so her home is like an embassy, ​​with cars like flowing water and horses like dragons in front of the door. One day, a group of guests came to Marlene Dietrich's house, including old and young, a whole family group. When they arrived at Marlene's house, they gathered in the square in the garden, the young ones brought wine and food, and arranged them on the grass; a group of people sat on the grass and picnicked, the children sat on the ground singing, and the older ones drank wine. Marlene's garden was actually used as a picnic place, but Marlene was very polite to them. Since then, Marlene Dietrich's hospitality has been talked about for a while in Hollywood. Many nosy people in Hollywood had to go to Marlene Dietrich's home every day for a visit, but now Marlene Dietrich has left Paramount, and the gate of her former residence is tightly closed, and no one can enter and play at will, which makes people feel a lot of vicissitudes.

Shen Xiling Receives Great Attention

Shen Xiling, the director of "A Woman's Cry," has decided to continue his directing work after three months of in-depth research. He has now selected a new script, "Shanghai Twenty-Four Hours," and will start filming immediately. The film is written by Cai Shusheng, and it depicts the general life of Shanghai society. It is very lively and profound. The female lead in the film has been decided to be Ms. Zhu Qiuhen, and Zhou Boxun, who starred in "Spring Dream of the Old Capital" at Lianhua, is said to play an important role in the film.

Zhang Shichuan Returns with a Full Load

Zhang Shichuan and Cheng Bugao, who have been running around in North China, Central China, and West China to film new films, have returned to Shanghai with their team last night because a part of their work has been completed. According to Ms. Xu Lai, a standard beauty, they have made nine films on this trip. Although they have tasted the hardships of long journeys, the results are very satisfactory, which can be said to be a worthwhile trip. According to the plan for the interior scenes of the film, it will be screened one after another within the year, so the Mingxing studio has been in a state of tension again in recent days.

Movie Novel

Mirage Three-Cornered Moon (3)

— Bolun

Mrs. Linbaga put on the airs of her in-laws and said, "Children, don't get too excited, or you will get nervous. And one thing, you have to sit down, because thinking while sitting is always better than thinking while standing." Elizabeth sighed. Kenna heard that he was studying law, and he should ask his mother about it. "Mother, when did you buy those stocks?" Mrs. Linbaga straightened her heavy body and said, "This is a long story. I'm left alone to take care of so many children. I was thinking of finding a way to get more money so that you can be happy in the future, so I took seventy-five thousand yuan to buy some stocks." Elizabeth screamed in shock, "Seventy-five thousand yuan." Mrs. Linbaga continued, "Later I added another fifty thousand. I'm not stupid, because someone told me that he was a very good person, and he said that Shuiyue Company's stock was the best." Kennas said, "What Shuiyue Company?" Mrs. Linbaga touched her head and said, "Let me think about it... it's probably a mine company, or a kind of metal mine... I think that person is very handsome, with a small mustache on his lips. He told me that Shuiyue Company's stock is very promising." Elizabeth interjected and asked, "What's that person's name?" Mrs. Linbaga said, "Let me think about it, this name was just on the tip of my tongue, how did I forget it for a while. His first name starts with S, um, Silver, no, it's not." Kennas said anxiously, "No matter what his name is. What happened after that?" Mrs. Linbaga said, "It was very good at first. Later it slowly fell. I thought it would rise. Later it really rose, but later it fell again, and later it rose again. I thought it wouldn't fall again this time. Who knew what I thought was right, it fell again, and it never climbed up again. Until a week ago, Mr. Bulizhi... now I remember, his name is Mr. Bulizhi, he told me to put some more money in. I gave him some more money, a lot of money. This morning he asked me to put money in again, but the money in the bank has been emptied." The four children asked together, "Then what happens?" Mrs. Linbaga said, "Then what happens?" I'm not a child, so I called a car and went home to wash my hair."

Elizabeth sighed, sat on the sofa, and held her head with both hands. The three children sat down one by one. Everyone was silent. Mrs. Linbaga was leisurely fanning herself, and in Lonad's room upstairs, the typewriter was making a da-da-da sound. Elizabeth suddenly thought of Dr. Stephen, who was a resourceful person and was good at giving people ideas. Whenever she met an accident, as long as he was by her side, she was not afraid of anything. "What do you do after you have no money?" This was the question she wanted to ask Stephen. How convenient, there was no need to ask, he came himself. Elizabeth had clearly heard his footsteps. Kennas was the first to speak, "Doctor, all our money is gone. Mother listened to a stranger and lost all the money!" Elizabeth heard this and jumped up angrily and said, "Are you saying this is all mother's fault? Aren't we all adults? Why didn't we know mother's temper earlier and take precautions?" (To be continued)
